<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149807173" id="p1" style="--height:145.677px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="6"></span>My dear brothers and sisters, welcome to general conference! I have looked forward to this day with great anticipation. I pray for you <em>every day</em>. I have also prayed that this conference will be a time of spiritual rejuvenation for each one of you.</p>
<p data-aid="149807174" id="p2" style="--height:144.01px;">Since last conference, difficulties in the world have continued. The global pandemic still affects our lives. And now the world has been rocked by a conflict that is raining terror on millions of innocent men, women, and children.</p>
<p data-aid="149807175" id="p12" style="--height:230.417px;">Prophets have foreseen our day, when there would be wars and rumors of wars and when the whole earth would be in commotion.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/11nelson?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a> As followers of Jesus Christ, we plead with leaders of nations to find peaceful resolutions to their differences. We call upon people everywhere to pray for those in need, to do what they can to help the distressed, and to seek the Lord’s help in ending any major conflicts.</p>
<p data-aid="149807176" id="p3" style="--height:174.479px;">Brothers and sisters, the gospel of Jesus Christ has never been needed more than it is today. Contention violates everything the Savior stood for and taught. I love the Lord Jesus Christ and testify that His gospel is the <em>only</em> enduring solution for peace. His gospel is a gospel of peace.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/11nelson?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807177" id="p5" style="--height:235.417px;">His gospel is the <em>only</em> answer when many in the world are stunned with fear.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/11nelson?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a> This underscores the urgent need for us to follow the Lord’s instruction to His disciples to “go … into <em>all</em> the world, and preach the gospel to <em>every</em> creature.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/11nelson?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a> We have the sacred responsibility to share the power and peace of Jesus Christ with all who will listen and who will let God prevail in their lives.</p>
<p data-aid="149807178" id="p6" style="--height:172.813px;">Every person who has made covenants with God has promised to care about others and serve those in need. We can demonstrate faith in God and always be ready to respond to those who ask about “the hope that is in [us].”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/11nelson?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a> Each of us has a role to play in the gathering of Israel.</p>
<p data-aid="149807179" id="p7" style="--height:232.083px;">Today I reaffirm strongly that the Lord has asked <em>every</em> worthy, able young man to prepare for and serve a mission. For Latter-day Saint young men, missionary service is a priesthood responsibility. You young men have been reserved for this time when the promised gathering of Israel is taking place. As you serve missions, you play a pivotal role in this unprecedented event!</p>
<p data-aid="149807180" id="p8" style="--height:203.281px;">For you young and able sisters, a mission is also a powerful, but <em>optional</em>, opportunity. We <em>love</em> sister missionaries and welcome them wholeheartedly. What you contribute to this work is magnificent! Pray to know if the Lord would have you serve a mission, and the Holy Ghost will respond to your heart and mind.</p>
<p data-aid="149807181" id="p9" style="--height:201.615px;">Dear young friends, you are each vital to the Lord. He has held you in reserve until now to help gather Israel. Your decision to serve a mission, whether a proselyting or a service mission, will bless you and <span class="page-break" data-page="7"></span>many others. We also welcome senior couples to serve when their circumstances permit. Their efforts are simply irreplaceable.</p>
<p data-aid="149807182" id="p10" style="--height:203.281px;"><em>All</em> missionaries teach and testify of the Savior. The spiritual darkness in the world makes the light of Jesus Christ needed more than ever. Everyone deserves the chance to know about the restored gospel of Jesus Christ. Every person deserves to know where they can find the hope and peace that “[pass] all understanding.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/11nelson?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807183" id="p11" style="--height:115.208px;">May this conference be a time of peace and spiritual feasting for you. May you seek and receive personal revelation during these sessions, I pray in the sacred name of Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149804948" id="p1" style="--height:57.6042px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="8"></span>Thank you, President Nelson, for sharing again that counsel regarding missionary service.</p>
<p data-aid="149804951" id="p2" style="--height:144.01px;">Brothers and sisters, several years ago while I was speaking in general conference, the sight in my left eye was suddenly compromised by something called macular degeneration, which subsequently worsened and has left me without useful vision in that eye.</p>
<p data-aid="149804953" id="p3" style="--height:230.417px;">As I have dealt with this challenge, I am ever more thankful for other kinds of vision, including hindsight vision. As I have looked back over my life, I have been able to see certain experiences that made a significant difference. One of those experiences is how my full-time missionary service as a young man in England blessed my life and shaped my spiritual destiny.</p>
<p data-aid="149804955" id="p4" style="--height:201.615px;">I have reflected on how the economic challenges associated with the Great Depression in the 1930s led to an unfortunate turn for my parents and our family. My father became so involved in saving his automobile dealership and supporting a family during this difficult period that for a time my parents did not attend church.</p>
<p data-aid="149804957" id="p5" style="--height:86.4063px;">Although we did not attend church services as a family, that did not prevent me from attending occasionally with my friends.</p>
<p data-aid="149804959" id="p6" style="--height:86.4063px;">In those days, going on a mission was in the back of my mind, but it wasn’t something I talked about with my parents.</p>
<p data-aid="149804961" id="p7" style="--height:230.417px;">While attending college, several friends and I decided to serve missions. Visiting with my bishop, I filled out my missionary application while my parents were out of town. When my parents returned, I surprised them with the news that I had been called to serve in Great Britain. I am grateful for their enthusiastic support of this decision and for good friends who helped me decide to serve.</p>
<p data-aid="149804963" id="p8" style="--height:115.208px;">My missionary service prepared me to be a better husband and father and to be successful in business. It also prepared me for a lifetime of service to the Lord in His Church.</p>
<p data-aid="149804965" id="p9" style="--height:230.417px;">In the April 1985 general conference, I was assigned to speak in the priesthood session. I directed my remarks to the young men. I spoke about preparing to serve as a missionary. I said, “Of all the training I have received in my Church assignments, none has been more important to me than the training I received as a nineteen-year-old elder serving a full-time mission.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/12ballard?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804966" id="p10" style="--height:230.417px;">The Lord knows you. When you are serving your mission, you will have <span class="page-break" data-page="9"></span>experiences that will help you come to know Him better. You will grow spiritually in serving Him. In His name, you will be sent on errands to serve others. He will give you experiences with promptings from the Holy Ghost. The Lord will authorize you to teach in His name. You can show Him that He can trust you and can rely on you.</p>
<p data-aid="149804968" id="p11" style="--height:230.417px;">Just over five months ago, Elder Jeffrey&nbsp;R. Holland and Elder Quentin&nbsp;L. Cook, who had also served as missionaries in the British Isles, joined me in visiting with members and missionaries in that beautiful land. While there, I reflected on my experiences as a young missionary. I testify that my mission is where I came to know that my Heavenly Father and my Savior, Jesus Christ, know and love me.</p>
<p data-aid="149804970" id="p12" style="--height:259.219px;">I was blessed to have two wonderful mission presidents, Selvoy&nbsp;J. Boyer and Stayner Richards, along with their dedicated companions, Gladys Boyer and Jane Richards. Looking back, I can see even more clearly that they trusted me and loved me. They taught me the gospel. They expected a lot from me. They gave me many challenging assignments and leadership responsibilities to help me to grow and prepare for a life of service.</p>
<p data-aid="149804971" id="p13" style="--height:518.438px;">I have also reflected on being called by President Spencer&nbsp;W. Kimball to preside over the Canada Toronto Mission with my dear wife, Barbara, and our children at our sides. President Kimball called us to serve in April 1974, shortly after he gave his inspired missionary message titled “When the World Will Be Converted.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/12ballard?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a> In that message President Kimball explained his vision for how the gospel would be taken to all the world. He called for many more missionaries from around the world. He reminded us of the Lord’s expectation “that every man should … lift a warning voice unto the inhabitants of the earth.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/12ballard?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a> President Kimball’s teaching about the expectation for young men to serve a mission became a topic of conversation in homes around the world. That expectation has not changed. I am grateful that President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson also reaffirmed the Lord’s expectation this morning.</p>
<p data-aid="149804973" id="p14" style="--height:172.813px;">It has been almost 10 years since President Thomas&nbsp;S. Monson announced the lowering of the missionary age for young men and young women.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/12ballard?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a> In my view, a primary reason for this change was to give more of our youth the life-changing opportunity to serve as a missionary.</p>
<p data-aid="149804975" id="p15" style="--height:201.615px;">As an Apostle of the Lord Jesus Christ, I now call upon you young men—and those young women who desire to serve a mission—to begin right now to talk with your parents about serving a mission. I also invite you to talk with your friends about serving a mission, and if one of your friends is not sure about serving, encourage them to talk with their bishop.</p>
<p data-aid="149804977" id="p16" style="--height:144.01px;">Commit to yourselves and to your Heavenly Father that you will serve a mission and that from this time forward you will strive to keep your hearts, hands, and minds clean and worthy. I invite you to gain a solid testimony of the restored gospel of Jesus Christ.</p>
<p data-aid="149804979" id="p17" style="--height:172.813px;">Fathers and mothers of these wonderful youth, you have a vital role in this preparation process. Begin today to talk with your children about missionary service. We know that the family is the most profound influence in helping our young men and young women prepare.</p>
<p data-aid="149804980" id="p18" style="--height:115.208px;">If you are still in the age range for missionary service but have not served yet due to the pandemic or other reasons, I invite you to serve now. Talk to your bishop, and prepare to serve the Lord.</p>
<p data-aid="149804983" id="p19" style="--height:201.615px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="10"></span>I encourage you bishops to help all young men and young women who are close to missionary age to prepare to serve, and I also encourage you bishops to identify those who are old enough but who have not yet served. Invite each young man to become a missionary, as well as each young woman who desires to serve.</p>
<p data-aid="149804986" id="p20" style="--height:403.229px;">To the missionaries currently serving, we thank you. Your mission has been during a worldwide pandemic. As a result, your mission experience has been unlike my mission experience or the experiences of any missionaries who served before 2020. I know it has not been easy. But even during these difficult times, the Lord has had a work for you to do, and you have done it wonderfully well. For example, you have used technology in new ways to find those who are ready to learn about the Restoration of the gospel of Jesus Christ. As you have served diligently and according to your abilities, I know that the Lord is pleased with your effort. I know that your service will bless your life.</p>
<p data-aid="149804988" id="p21" style="--height:201.615px;">When you are released from your mission, remember that you are not released from activity in the Church. Build upon the good habits you learned on your mission, continue to strengthen your testimony, work hard, pray, and be obedient to the Lord. Honor the covenants you have made. Continue to bless and serve others.</p>
<p data-aid="149804990" id="p22" style="--height:288.021px;">I pray that you young men and young women and your parents will see and know how missionary service will forever bless your life. May you know in your minds and feel in your hearts the power of the invitation the Lord gave to the great missionary sons of Mosiah. He said, “Go forth … and establish my word; yet ye shall be patient in long-suffering and afflictions, that ye may show forth good examples … in me, and I will make an instrument of thee in my hands unto the salvation of many souls.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/12ballard?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804992" id="p23" style="--height:115.208px;">May God bless the youth of the Church to desire to prepare and serve Him is my humble prayer, which I offer this morning in the sacred name of the Lord Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149804956" id="p1" style="--height:345.625px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="11"></span>After receiving an invitation to “come and see,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a> I attended The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints for the first time at the age of 26. I had recently separated from my first husband. I had a three-year-old boy. And I felt powerless with fear. When I entered the building, I was filled with warmth as I perceived the faith and joy of the people surrounding me. It was truly “a refuge from the storm.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a> Three weeks later, I made the baptismal covenant with Heavenly Father and started my journey as a disciple of Christ, although my life has not been perfect along that journey.</p>
<p data-aid="149804958" id="p2" style="--height:288.021px;">For me to receive those eternal blessings, many physical and spiritual elements had to be in place. The gospel of Jesus Christ had been restored and preached; that meetinghouse had been built and maintained; there was an ecclesiastical structure, from the prophet to local leaders; and a branch filled by covenant members was ready to embrace me and my son as we were brought to the Savior, “nourished by the good word of God,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a> and given opportunities to serve.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804960" id="p3" style="--height:374.427px;">From the beginning, God has sought to gather and organize His children<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a> “to bring to pass [our] immortality and eternal life.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a> With that purpose in mind, He has instructed us to build places of worship<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a> where we receive knowledge and the ordinances of salvation and exaltation; make and keep covenants that bind us to Jesus Christ;<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note8" data-scroll-id="note8"><sup class="marker">8</sup></a> are endowed with “the power of godliness”;<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note9" data-scroll-id="note9"><sup class="marker">9</sup></a> and gather together often to remember Jesus and strengthen each other in Him.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note10" data-scroll-id="note10"><sup class="marker">10</sup></a> The Church organization and its buildings exist for our spiritual benefit. “The Church … is the scaffolding with which we build eternal families.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note11" data-scroll-id="note11"><sup class="marker">11</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804962" id="p4" style="--height:288.021px;">While talking to a friend going through a difficult time, I asked how he was surviving financially. In tears, he replied that his bishop was helping him using fast-offering funds. He added, “I don’t know where my family and I would be if it wasn’t for the Church.” I replied, “The Church is the <em>members</em>. They are the ones who willingly and joyfully give fast offerings to help those of us in need. You are receiving the fruits of their faith and determination to follow Jesus Christ.”</p>
<p data-aid="149804964" id="p5" style="--height:201.615px;">My fellow disciples of Christ, let us not underestimate the marvelous work the Lord is doing through <em>us</em>, His Church, despite our shortcomings. Sometimes we are givers and sometimes we are receivers, but we are all one family in Christ. His Church is the structure He has given to guide and bless us as we worship Him and serve each other.</p>
<p data-aid="149804967" id="p6" style="--height:201.615px;">Some sisters have apologized to me, thinking they are not active members of Relief Society because they are serving in Primary or Young Women. Those sisters are among the <span class="page-break" data-page="12"></span>most active members of Relief Society because they are helping our precious children and youth strengthen their faith in Jesus Christ.</p>
<p data-aid="149804969" id="p7" style="--height:345.625px;">Relief Society is not limited to a room in a building, a Sunday lesson, an activity, or a presidency at the local or general level. Relief Society is the covenant women of the Church; it is <em>us</em>—<em>each of us</em> and <em>all of us</em>. It is our “global community of compassion and service.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note12" data-scroll-id="note12"><sup class="marker">12</sup></a> Anywhere and everywhere we go, we are always part of Relief Society as we strive to fulfill its divine purpose, which is for women to accomplish God’s work in individual as well as collective ways<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note13" data-scroll-id="note13"><sup class="marker">13</sup></a> by providing relief: “relief of poverty, relief of illness; relief of doubt, relief of ignorance—relief of all that hinders … joy and progress.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note14" data-scroll-id="note14"><sup class="marker">14</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804972" id="p8" style="--height:230.417px;">Similar belonging exists in elders quorums and organizations of the Church for all ages, including our children and youth. The Church is more than the buildings and the ecclesiastical structure; the Church is <em>us</em>, the members. <em>We</em> are The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints, with Christ at the head and the prophet as His mouthpiece. The Lord has said:</p>
<p data-aid="149804974" id="p9" style="--height:57.6042px;">“Behold, this is my doctrine—whosoever repenteth and cometh unto me, the same is my church.&nbsp;…</p>
<p data-aid="149804976" id="p10" style="--height:86.4063px;">“And … whosoever is of my church, and endureth of my church to the end, him will I establish upon my rock.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note15" data-scroll-id="note15"><sup class="marker">15</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804978" id="p11" style="--height:172.813px;">Sisters and brothers, let us realize how privileged we are to belong to the Church of Jesus Christ, where we can unite our faith, hearts, strengths, minds, and hands for Him to perform His mighty miracles. “For the body [of Christ’s Church] is not one member, but many.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note16" data-scroll-id="note16"><sup class="marker">16</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804981" id="p12" style="--height:115.208px;">A teenage boy told his mother, “When I was little, every time I gave one dollar in tithing, I thought that with that <em>one</em> dollar a <em>whole</em> meetinghouse would be built. Isn’t that silly?”</p>
<p data-aid="149804982" id="p13" style="--height:57.6042px;">Touched, she replied, “That is lovely! Did you picture them in your mind?”</p>
<p data-aid="149804984" id="p14" style="--height:57.6042px;">“Yes!” he exclaimed. “They were beautiful, and there were millions of them!”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note17" data-scroll-id="note17"><sup class="marker">17</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804985" id="p15" style="--height:86.4063px;">My dear friends, let us have the faith of a child and rejoice in knowing that even our smallest efforts are making a significant difference in God’s kingdom.</p>
<p data-aid="149804987" id="p16" style="--height:86.4063px;">Our purpose in His kingdom should be to bring each other to Christ. As we read in the scriptures, the Savior extended this invitation to the Nephites:</p>
<p data-aid="149804989" id="p17" style="--height:144.01px;">“Have ye any that are sick among you? Bring them hither. Have ye any that are … afflicted in any manner? Bring them hither and I will heal them, for I have compassion upon you; my bowels are filled with mercy.</p>
<p data-aid="149804991" id="p18" style="--height:57.6042px;">“…&nbsp;I see that your faith is sufficient that I should heal you.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note18" data-scroll-id="note18"><sup class="marker">18</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149804993" id="p19" style="--height:172.813px;">Do we not all have afflictions that can be brought to the Savior’s feet? While some of us have physical challenges, many more battle with emotional strife, others struggle to nurture social connections, and we <span class="page-break" data-page="13"></span>all seek respite when our spirits are challenged. We are <em>all</em> afflicted in some manner.</p>
<p data-aid="149804997" id="p20" style="--height:115.208px;">We read that “all the multitude, with one accord, did go forth with their sick and … with <em>all</em> them that were afflicted in any manner; and he <em>did</em> heal them <em>every one</em> as they were brought forth unto him.</p>
<p data-aid="149805001" id="p21" style="--height:86.4063px;">“And they did all, both they who had been healed and they who were whole, bow down at his feet, and did worship him.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note19" data-scroll-id="note19"><sup class="marker">19</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805003" id="p22" style="--height:230.417px;">From a little boy who pays tithing with faith, to a single mother in need of the Lord’s empowering grace, to a father struggling to provide for his family, to our ancestors in need of the ordinances of salvation and exaltation, to each of us who renews covenants with God every week, we need each other, and we can bring each other to the Savior’s redeeming healing.</p>
<p data-aid="149805006" id="p23" style="--height:144.01px;">My dear sisters and brothers, let us follow Jesus Christ’s invitation to bring ourselves and our afflictions to Him. When we come to Him and bring those we love to Him, He sees our faith. He will make them whole, and He will make us whole.</p>
<p data-aid="149805007" id="p24" style="--height:230.417px;">As “the peaceable followers of Christ,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note20" data-scroll-id="note20"><sup class="marker">20</sup></a> we are striving to become “of one heart and one mind”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note21" data-scroll-id="note21"><sup class="marker">21</sup></a> and to be humble; submissive; gentle; easy to be entreated; full of patience and long-suffering; temperate in all things; diligent in keeping the commandments of God at all times; full of faith, hope, and charity; and abounding in good works.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note22" data-scroll-id="note22"><sup class="marker">22</sup></a> We are striving to become like Jesus Christ.</p>
<p data-aid="149805009" id="p25" style="--height:144.01px;">I testify that as Christ’s Church, we are the means through which, as President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson taught, “our Savior and Redeemer, Jesus Christ, will perform some of His mightiest works between now and when He comes again.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note23" data-scroll-id="note23"><sup class="marker">23</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805011" id="p26" style="--height:28.8021px;">The Lord has said:</p>
<p data-aid="149805013" id="p27" style="--height:28.8021px;">“Behold, I will hasten my work in its time.</p>
<p data-aid="149805015" id="p28" style="--height:172.813px;">“And I give unto you … a commandment that you assemble yourselves together, and organize yourselves, and prepare yourselves, and sanctify yourselves; yea, purify your hearts, and cleanse your hands and your feet before me, that I may make you clean.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/13aburto?lang=eng#note24" data-scroll-id="note24"><sup class="marker">24</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805017" id="p29" style="--height:86.4063px;">May we respond to this divine invitation and joyfully assemble, organize, prepare, and sanctify ourselves is my humble prayer in the name of Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149807198" id="p1" style="--height:259.219px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="14"></span>My wife, Susan, our three sons and their wives, all of our grandchildren, and Elder Quentin&nbsp;L. Cook, my seatmate in the Quorum of the Twelve for almost 15 years, all readily will attest to the fact that I do not sing well. But in spite of my lack of vocal talent, I love to sing the hymns of the Restoration. The combination of inspired lyrics and majestic melodies helps me to learn essential gospel principles and stirs my soul.</p>
<p data-aid="149807200" id="p2" style="--height:144.01px;">One hymn that has blessed my life in remarkable ways is “Let Us All Press On.” Recently I have been pondering and learning about a specific phrase in the refrain of that hymn. “<em>We will heed not</em> what the wicked may say, but the Lord alone we will obey.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a> </p>
<p data-aid="149807202" id="p3" style="--height:28.8021px;"><em>We will heed not</em>.</p>
<p data-aid="149807204" id="p4" style="--height:316.823px;">As I sing “Let Us All Press On,” I often think of the people in Lehi’s vision pressing forward on the path that led to the tree of life who were not merely “clinging to”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a> but were “continually holding fast to the rod of iron, until they came forth and fell down and partook of the fruit of the tree.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a> Lehi described multitudes in the great and spacious building that were pointing “the finger of scorn at [him] and those … partaking of the fruit.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a> His response to the jeers and insults is magnificent and memorable: “<em>But we heeded them not</em>.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a> </p>
<p data-aid="149807206" id="p5" style="--height:144.01px;">I pray that the Holy Ghost will bless and enlighten each of us as we consider together how we can be strengthened to “heed not” the evil influences and mocking voices of the contemporary world in which we live.</p>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807209" id="title2" style="--height:33.6111px;">Heed Not </h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807210" id="p6" style="--height:259.219px;">The word <em>heed</em> suggests taking notice of or paying attention to someone or something. Thus, the lyrics of the hymn “Let Us All Press On” admonish us to make an affirmative decision to pay no attention to “what the wicked may say.” And Lehi and the people with him who were partaking of the fruit of the tree provide a strong example of not paying attention to the mocking and scorn that so frequently come from the great and spacious building.</p>
<p data-aid="149807213" id="p7" style="--height:374.427px;">The doctrine of Christ written “with the Spirit of the living God … in fleshy tables of [our hearts]”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a> increases our capacity to “heed not” the many distractions, taunts, and diversions in our fallen world. For example, faith focused in and on the Lord Jesus Christ fortifies us with spiritual strength. Faith in the Redeemer is a principle of action and of power. As we act in accordance with the truths of His gospel, we are blessed with the spiritual capacity to press forward through the challenges of mortality while focusing on the joys the Savior offers to us. Truly, “if we do what’s right we have no need to fear, for the Lord, our helper, will ever be near.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807216" id="title3" style="--height:67.2222px;">A Personal Connection through Covenants </h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807220" id="p8" style="--height:288.021px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="15"></span>Entering into sacred covenants and worthily receiving priesthood ordinances yoke us with and bind us to the Lord Jesus Christ and Heavenly Father.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note8" data-scroll-id="note8"><sup class="marker">8</sup></a> This simply means that we trust in the Savior as our Advocate<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note9" data-scroll-id="note9"><sup class="marker">9</sup></a> and Mediator<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note10" data-scroll-id="note10"><sup class="marker">10</sup></a> and rely on His merits, mercy, and grace<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note11" data-scroll-id="note11"><sup class="marker">11</sup></a> during the journey of life. As we are steadfast in coming unto Christ and are yoked with Him, we receive the cleansing, healing, and strengthening blessings of His infinite and eternal Atonement.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note12" data-scroll-id="note12"><sup class="marker">12</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807223" id="p9" style="--height:288.021px;">Living and loving covenant commitments creates a connection with the Lord that is deeply personal and spiritually powerful. As we honor the conditions of sacred covenants and ordinances, we gradually and incrementally are drawn closer to Him<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note13" data-scroll-id="note13"><sup class="marker">13</sup></a> and experience the impact of His divinity and living reality in our lives. Jesus then becomes much more than the central character in scripture stories; His example and teachings influence our every desire, thought, and action. </p>
<p data-aid="149807226" id="p10" style="--height:345.625px;">I frankly do not have the ability to describe adequately the precise nature and power of our covenant connection with the resurrected and living Son of God. But I witness that the connections with Him and Heavenly Father are real and are the ultimate sources of assurance, peace, joy, and the spiritual strength that enable us to “fear not, though the enemy deride.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note14" data-scroll-id="note14"><sup class="marker">14</sup></a> As covenant-making and covenant-keeping disciples of Jesus Christ, we can be blessed to take “courage, for the Lord is on our side”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note15" data-scroll-id="note15"><sup class="marker">15</sup></a> and pay no attention to evil influences and secular scoffing.</p>
<p data-aid="149807229" id="p11" style="--height:115.208px;">As I visit with members of the Church around the world, I often ask them this question: what helps you to “heed not” worldly influences, mocking, and scorn? Their answers are most instructive.</p>
<p data-aid="149807231" id="p12" style="--height:316.823px;">Valiant members often highlight the importance of inviting the power of the Holy Ghost into their lives through meaningful scripture study, fervent prayer, and proper preparation to participate in the ordinance of the sacrament. Also mentioned frequently are the spiritual support of faithful family members and trusted friends, the vital lessons learned through ministering and serving in the Lord’s restored Church, and the capacity to discern the absolute emptiness of anything in or coming from the great and spacious building. </p>
<p data-aid="149807234" id="p13" style="--height:374.427px;">I have noted in these member responses a particular pattern that is especially significant. First and foremost, these disciples have firm testimonies of Heavenly Father’s plan of happiness and the role of Jesus Christ as our Redeemer and Savior. And second, their spiritual knowledge and conviction are individual, personal, and specific; they are not general and abstract. I listen to these devoted souls speak of covenants providing strength to overcome opposition and their connection with the living Lord supporting them through times both good and bad. To these individuals, Jesus Christ indeed is a personal Savior.</p>
<div><div class="imageWrapper-wTPPD"><figure class="imageWithModal-bCN6D loadImageItem-u5D4D" title="Christus"><img width="500" height="323" alt=""><div class="container-W4jed"><div class="innerFlex-R9N_u"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" role="presentation" style="width: 1.5rem; height: 1.5rem;"> <path fill="currentColor" d="M20 4.75L19.25 4v16l.75-.75H4l.75.75V4L4 4.75h16zM3.25 4v16c0 .414.336.75.75.75h16a.75.75 0 0 0 .75-.75V4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75-.75H4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75.75zm11.07 8.888c.23-.357.606-.353.828-.008l2.887 4.482c.227.352.06.638-.357.638H6.326c-.421 0-.581-.3-.37-.648l4.006-6.622c.217-.358.567-.359.793.014l2.396 3.96 1.17-1.816zm1.59-2.735c1.14 0 2.066-.907 2.066-2.026 0-1.12-.926-2.027-2.067-2.027s-2.066.907-2.066 2.027c0 1.119.925 2.026 2.066 2.026z"> </path></svg><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr i18nString-raclU">Image</div><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr title-RrK9J">Christus</div></div></div></figure></div></div>
<p data-aid="149807238" id="p14" style="--height:230.417px;">Gospel covenants and ordinances operate in our lives much like a compass. A compass is a device used to indicate the cardinal directions of north, south, east, and west for purposes of navigation and geographic orientation. In a similar way, our covenants and ordinances point us to and help us always remember our connection with the Lord Jesus Christ as we progress along the covenant path. </p>
<div><div class="imageWrapper-wTPPD"><figure class="imageWithModal-bCN6D loadImageItem-u5D4D" title="Christus"><img width="500" height="323" alt=""><div class="container-W4jed"><div class="innerFlex-R9N_u"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" role="presentation" style="width: 1.5rem; height: 1.5rem;"> <path fill="currentColor" d="M20 4.75L19.25 4v16l.75-.75H4l.75.75V4L4 4.75h16zM3.25 4v16c0 .414.336.75.75.75h16a.75.75 0 0 0 .75-.75V4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75-.75H4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75.75zm11.07 8.888c.23-.357.606-.353.828-.008l2.887 4.482c.227.352.06.638-.357.638H6.326c-.421 0-.581-.3-.37-.648l4.006-6.622c.217-.358.567-.359.793.014l2.396 3.96 1.17-1.816zm1.59-2.735c1.14 0 2.066-.907 2.066-2.026 0-1.12-.926-2.027-2.067-2.027s-2.066.907-2.066 2.027c0 1.119.925 2.026 2.066 2.026z"> </path></svg><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr i18nString-raclU">Image</div><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr title-RrK9J">Christus</div></div></div></figure></div></div>
<p data-aid="149807240" id="p15" style="--height:201.615px;">The cardinal direction for all of us in mortality is to come unto and be perfected in Christ.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note16" data-scroll-id="note16"><sup class="marker">16</sup></a> Holy covenants and ordinances help us to keep our focus upon the Savior and strive, with His grace,<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note17" data-scroll-id="note17"><sup class="marker">17</sup></a> to become more like Him. Most assuredly, “an unseen [power] will aid me and you in the glorious cause of truth.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note18" data-scroll-id="note18"><sup class="marker">18</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807243" id="title4" style="--height:33.6111px;">Holding Fast to the Iron Rod</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807246" id="p16" style="--height:172.813px;">Our covenant connection with God and Jesus Christ is the channel through which we can receive the capacity and strength to “heed not.” And this bond is strengthened as we continually hold fast to the rod of iron. But as Nephi’s brethren asked, “What meaneth the rod of iron which our father saw&nbsp;…&nbsp;?</p>
<p data-aid="149807249" id="p17" style="--height:172.813px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="16"></span>“And [Nephi] said unto them that it was the <em>word of God</em>; and whoso would hearken unto <em>the word of God</em>, and would <em>hold fast unto it</em>, they would never perish; neither could the temptations and the fiery darts of the adversary overpower them unto blindness, to lead them away to destruction.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note19" data-scroll-id="note19"><sup class="marker">19</sup></a> </p>
<p data-aid="149807252" id="p18" style="--height:115.208px;">Please note that the ability to resist the temptations and the fiery darts of the adversary is promised to those individuals who “hold fast to” rather than merely “cling to” the word of God.</p>
<p data-aid="149807257" id="p19" style="--height:57.6042px;">Interestingly, the Apostle John described Jesus Christ as the Word.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note20" data-scroll-id="note20"><sup class="marker">20</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807262" id="p20" style="--height:57.6042px;">“In the beginning was <em>the Word</em>, and <em>the Word</em> was with God, and <em>the Word</em> was God.&nbsp;…</p>
<p data-aid="149807266" id="p21" style="--height:57.6042px;">“All things were made by him; and without him was not any thing made that was made.&nbsp;…</p>
<p data-aid="149807270" id="p22" style="--height:86.4063px;">“And <em>the Word</em> was made flesh, and dwelt among us, (and we beheld his glory, the glory as of the only begotten of the Father,) full of grace and truth.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note21" data-scroll-id="note21"><sup class="marker">21</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807274" id="p23" style="--height:57.6042px;">Therefore, one of the names of Jesus Christ is “The Word.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note22" data-scroll-id="note22"><sup class="marker">22</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807278" id="p24" style="--height:115.208px;">In addition, the <a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/pgp/a-of-f/1.8?lang=eng#p8">eighth article of faith</a> states, “We believe the Bible to be <em>the word of God</em> as far as it is translated correctly; we also believe the Book of Mormon to be <em>the word of God</em>.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note23" data-scroll-id="note23"><sup class="marker">23</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807282" id="p25" style="--height:57.6042px;">Thus, the teachings of the Savior, as recorded in the holy scriptures, also are “the word.” </p>
<p data-aid="149807286" id="p26" style="--height:432.031px;">Let me suggest that holding fast to the word of God entails (1)&nbsp;remembering, honoring, and strengthening the personal connection we have with the Savior and His Father through the covenants and ordinances of the restored gospel and (2)&nbsp;prayerfully, earnestly, and consistently using the holy scriptures and the teachings of living prophets and apostles as sure sources of revealed truth. As we are bound and “hold fast” to the Lord and are transformed by living His doctrine,<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note24" data-scroll-id="note24"><sup class="marker">24</sup></a> I promise that individually and collectively we will be blessed to “stand in holy places, and shall not be moved.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note25" data-scroll-id="note25"><sup class="marker">25</sup></a> If we abide in Christ, then He will abide in and walk with us.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note26" data-scroll-id="note26"><sup class="marker">26</sup></a> Surely, “in the days of trial his Saints he will cheer, and prosper the cause of truth.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note27" data-scroll-id="note27"><sup class="marker">27</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807290" id="title5" style="--height:33.6111px;">Testimony</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807294" id="p27" style="--height:28.8021px;">Press on. Hold fast. Heed not.</p>
<p data-aid="149807298" id="p28" style="--height:201.615px;">I witness that fidelity to the covenants and ordinances of the Savior’s restored gospel enables us to <em>press on</em> in the work of the Lord, to <em>hold fast</em> to Him as the Word of God, and to <em>heed not</em> the allurements of the adversary. In the fight for right, may each of us wield a sword, even “the mighty sword of truth,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/14bednar?lang=eng#note28" data-scroll-id="note28"><sup class="marker">28</sup></a> in the sacred name of the Lord Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</section>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149807207" id="p1" style="--height:201.615px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="17"></span>My dear brothers and sisters, as we experience sobering days of commotion, contention, and, for many, deep suffering, our hearts are filled with overwhelming gratitude for our Savior and the eternal blessings of the restored gospel of Jesus Christ. We love Him and we trust Him, and we pray that we will forever follow Him.</p>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807208" id="title2" style="--height:33.6111px;">The Challenge of Social Media</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807212" id="p2" style="--height:57.6042px;">The powerful impact of the internet is a blessing and a challenge, unique to our time.</p>
<p data-aid="149807214" id="p3" style="--height:144.01px;">In a world of social media and information superhighways, one person’s voice can be multiplied exponentially. That voice, whether true or false, whether fair or prejudicial, whether kind or cruel, moves instantly across the world.</p>
<p data-aid="149807217" id="p4" style="--height:230.417px;">Social media posts of thoughtfulness and goodness are often quietly under the radar, while words of contempt and anger are frequently thundering in our ears, whether with political philosophy, people in the news, or opinions on the pandemic. No one or no subject, including the Savior and His restored gospel, is immune from this social phenomenon of polarized voices.</p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807219" id="title3" style="--height:33.6111px;">Becoming a Peacemaker</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807222" id="p5" style="--height:86.4063px;">The Sermon on the Mount is a message for all but was specifically given to the Savior’s disciples, those who had chosen to follow Him.</p>
<p data-aid="149807225" id="p6" style="--height:115.208px;">The Lord taught how to live, then and now, in a contemptuous world. “Blessed are the peacemakers,” He declared, “for they shall be called the children of God.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807227" id="p7" style="--height:86.4063px;">By the shield of our faith in Jesus Christ, we become peacemakers, quenching—meaning to calm, cool, <span class="page-break" data-page="18"></span>or extinguish—all the fiery darts of the adversary.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807230" id="p8" style="--height:230.417px;">As we do our part, His promise is that we will be called the “children of God.” Every person on earth is the “offspring”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a> of God, but to be called the “children of God” means much, much more. As we come unto Jesus Christ and make covenants with Him, we become “his seed” and “heirs of the kingdom,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a> “children of Christ, his sons, and his daughters.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807233" id="p9" style="--height:144.01px;">How does a peacemaker calm and cool the fiery darts? Certainly not by shrinking before those who disparage us. Rather, we remain confident in our faith, sharing our beliefs with conviction but always void of anger or malice.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807236" id="p10" style="--height:144.01px;">Recently, after seeing a strongly worded opinion piece that was critical of the Church, Reverend Amos&nbsp;C. Brown, a national civil rights leader and pastor of the Third Baptist Church in San Francisco, responded:</p>
<p data-aid="149807239" id="p44" style="--height:86.4063px;">“I respect the experience and perspective of the individual who wrote those words. Granted, I don’t see what he sees.”</p>
<p data-aid="149807242" id="p45" style="--height:144.01px;">“I count it one of my life’s greatest joys to know these leaders [of the Church], including President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson. They are, in my estimation, the embodiment of the best leadership our country has to offer.”</p>
<div><div class="imageWrapper-wTPPD"><figure class="imageWithModal-bCN6D loadImageItem-u5D4D" title="First Presidency and NAACP Leaders Announce a Shared Vision to “Learn from and Serve One Another”"><img width="500" height="323" alt=""><div class="container-W4jed"><div class="innerFlex-R9N_u"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" role="presentation" style="width: 1.5rem; height: 1.5rem;"> <path fill="currentColor" d="M20 4.75L19.25 4v16l.75-.75H4l.75.75V4L4 4.75h16zM3.25 4v16c0 .414.336.75.75.75h16a.75.75 0 0 0 .75-.75V4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75-.75H4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75.75zm11.07 8.888c.23-.357.606-.353.828-.008l2.887 4.482c.227.352.06.638-.357.638H6.326c-.421 0-.581-.3-.37-.648l4.006-6.622c.217-.358.567-.359.793.014l2.396 3.96 1.17-1.816zm1.59-2.735c1.14 0 2.066-.907 2.066-2.026 0-1.12-.926-2.027-2.067-2.027s-2.066.907-2.066 2.027c0 1.119.925 2.026 2.066 2.026z"> </path></svg><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr i18nString-raclU">Image</div><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr title-RrK9J">First Presidency and NAACP Leaders Announce a Shared Vision to “Learn from and Serve One Another”</div></div></div></figure></div></div>
<p data-aid="149807245" id="p46" style="--height:201.615px;">He then added: “We can gripe about the way things were. We can refuse to acknowledge all the good going on now. … But these approaches will not heal our national divisions. … As Jesus taught, we don’t eradicate evil with more evil. We love generously and live mercifully, even toward those we think to be our enemies.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807248" id="p11" style="--height:86.4063px;">Reverend Brown is a peacemaker. He calmly and respectfully cooled the fiery darts. Peacemakers are not passive; they are persuasive in the Savior’s way.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note8" data-scroll-id="note8"><sup class="marker">8</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807250" id="p12" style="--height:115.208px;">What gives us the inner strength to cool, calm, and quench the fiery darts aimed toward the truths we love? The strength comes from our faith in Jesus Christ and our faith in His words.</p>
<p data-aid="149807253" id="p13" style="--height:86.4063px;">“Blessed are ye, when men shall revile you, … and shall say all manner of evil against you falsely, for my sake.</p>
<p data-aid="149807255" id="p39" style="--height:86.4063px;">“… For great is your reward in heaven: for so persecuted they the prophets which were before you.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note9" data-scroll-id="note9"><sup class="marker">9</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807258" id="title4" style="--height:33.6111px;">The Importance of Agency</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807261" id="p14" style="--height:57.6042px;">Two important principles guide our desire to be peacemakers.</p>
<p data-aid="149807265" id="p15" style="--height:115.208px;">First, our Heavenly Father has given each individual his or her moral <span class="page-break" data-page="19"></span>agency, with the ability to choose one’s own path.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note10" data-scroll-id="note10"><sup class="marker">10</sup></a> This agency is one of the greatest gifts of God.</p>
<p data-aid="149807269" id="p16" style="--height:144.01px;">Second, with this agency, our Heavenly Father allowed for “opposition in all things.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note11" data-scroll-id="note11"><sup class="marker">11</sup></a> We “taste the bitter, that [we] may know to prize the good.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note12" data-scroll-id="note12"><sup class="marker">12</sup></a> Opposition should not surprise us. We learn to distinguish good from evil.</p>
<p data-aid="149807273" id="p17" style="--height:144.01px;">We rejoice in the blessing of agency, understanding that there will be many who do not believe what we believe. In fact, few in the latter days will choose to make their faith in Jesus Christ central to all they think and do.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note13" data-scroll-id="note13"><sup class="marker">13</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807277" id="p18" style="--height:115.208px;">Because of social media platforms, one voice of disbelief can appear to be a multitude of negative voices,<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note14" data-scroll-id="note14"><sup class="marker">14</sup></a> but even if it is a multitude of voices, we choose the path of peacemakers.</p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807279" id="title5" style="--height:33.6111px;">The Lord’s Leaders</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807283" id="p19" style="--height:86.4063px;">Some view the First Presidency and the Quorum of the Twelve as having worldly motives, like political, business, and cultural leaders.</p>
<p data-aid="149807287" id="p20" style="--height:288.021px;">However, we come very differently to our responsibilities. We are not elected or selected from applications. Without any specific professional preparation, we are called and ordained to bear testimony of the name of Jesus Christ throughout the world until our final breath. We endeavor to bless the sick, the lonely, the downhearted, and the poor and to strengthen the kingdom of God. We seek to know the Lord’s will and to proclaim it, especially to those who seek eternal life.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note15" data-scroll-id="note15"><sup class="marker">15</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807291" id="p21" style="--height:144.01px;">Although our humble desire is for the Savior’s teachings to be honored by all, the words of the Lord through His prophets are often contrary to the thinking and trends of the world. It has always been so.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note16" data-scroll-id="note16"><sup class="marker">16</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807295" id="p22" style="--height:28.8021px;">The Savior said to His Apostles:</p>
<p data-aid="149807299" id="p40" style="--height:57.6042px;">“If the world [hates] you, ye know that it hated me before it hated you.&nbsp;…</p>
<p data-aid="149807303" id="p41" style="--height:57.6042px;">“… All these things will they do … because <em>they know not him</em> that sent me.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note17" data-scroll-id="note17"><sup class="marker">17</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807307" id="title6" style="--height:33.6111px;">Caring for All</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807308" id="p23" style="--height:172.813px;">We genuinely love and care for all our neighbors, whether or not they believe as we do. Jesus taught us in the parable of the Good Samaritan that those of different beliefs should sincerely reach out to help anyone in need, being peacemakers, pursuing good and noble causes.</p>
<p data-aid="149807310" id="p24" style="--height:86.4063px;">In February, a headline in the <em>Arizona Republic</em> stated, “Bipartisan bill supported by Latter-day Saints would protect gay and transgender Arizonans.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note18" data-scroll-id="note18"><sup class="marker">18</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807315" id="p25" style="--height:115.208px;">We, as Latter-day Saints, are “pleased to be part of a coalition of faith, business, LGBTQ people and community leaders who have worked together in a spirit of trust and mutual respect.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note19" data-scroll-id="note19"><sup class="marker">19</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807319" id="p26" style="--height:86.4063px;">President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson once thoughtfully asked, “Cannot boundary lines exist without becoming battle lines?”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note20" data-scroll-id="note20"><sup class="marker">20</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807325" id="p27" style="--height:28.8021px;">We endeavor to be “peaceable followers of Christ.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note21" data-scroll-id="note21"><sup class="marker">21</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807329" id="title7" style="--height:33.6111px;">The Times Not to Respond</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807331" id="p28" style="--height:201.615px;">Some of the attacks upon the Savior were so malicious that He said nothing. “And the chief priests and scribes … vehemently accused him … and mocked him,” but Jesus “answered [them] nothing.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note22" data-scroll-id="note22"><sup class="marker">22</sup></a> There are times when being a peacemaker means that we resist the impulse to respond and instead, with dignity, remain quiet.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note23" data-scroll-id="note23"><sup class="marker">23</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807337" id="p29" style="--height:172.813px;">It is heartbreaking for all of us when harsh or dismissive words about the Savior, His followers, and His Church are spoken or published by those who once stood with us, took the sacrament with us, and testified with us of the divine mission of Jesus Christ.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note24" data-scroll-id="note24"><sup class="marker">24</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807339" id="p30" style="--height:28.8021px;">This also happened during the Savior’s ministry.</p>
<p data-aid="149807344" id="p31" style="--height:144.01px;">Some of the disciples of Jesus who were with Him during His most majestic miracles determined to “[walk] no more with him.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note25" data-scroll-id="note25"><sup class="marker">25</sup></a> Sadly, not all will remain firm in their love for the Savior and their determination to keep His commandments.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note26" data-scroll-id="note26"><sup class="marker">26</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807349" id="p32" style="--height:201.615px;">Jesus taught us to withdraw from the circle of anger and contention. In one example, after the Pharisees confronted Jesus and counseled how they might destroy Him, the scriptures say that Jesus withdrew Himself from them,<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note27" data-scroll-id="note27"><sup class="marker">27</sup></a> and miracles occurred as “great multitudes followed him, and he healed them all.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note28" data-scroll-id="note28"><sup class="marker">28</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807354" id="title8" style="--height:33.6111px;">Blessing the Lives of Others</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807357" id="p33" style="--height:86.4063px;">We too can move away from contention and bless the lives of others<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note29" data-scroll-id="note29"><sup class="marker">29</sup></a> while not isolating ourselves in our own corner.</p>
<p data-aid="149807362" id="p34" style="--height:86.4063px;">In Mbuji-Mayi, Democratic Republic of the Congo, initially some were critical of the Church, not <span class="page-break" data-page="20"></span>understanding our beliefs or knowing our members.</p>
<p data-aid="149807365" id="p35" style="--height:316.823px;">Some time ago, Kathy and I attended a very special Church service in Mbuji-Mayi. The children were dressed immaculately, with bright eyes and big smiles. I had hoped to speak to them about their education but learned that many were not attending school. Our leaders, with very nominal humanitarian funds, found a way to help.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note30" data-scroll-id="note30"><sup class="marker">30</sup></a> Now, more than 400 students—girls and boys, members as well as those not of our faith—are welcomed and taught by 16 teachers who are members of the Church of Jesus Christ.</p>
<div><div class="imageWrapper-wTPPD"><figure class="imageWithModal-bCN6D loadImageItem-u5D4D" title="Kalanga Muya"><img width="500" height="323" alt=""><div class="container-W4jed"><div class="innerFlex-R9N_u"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" role="presentation" style="width: 1.5rem; height: 1.5rem;"> <path fill="currentColor" d="M20 4.75L19.25 4v16l.75-.75H4l.75.75V4L4 4.75h16zM3.25 4v16c0 .414.336.75.75.75h16a.75.75 0 0 0 .75-.75V4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75-.75H4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75.75zm11.07 8.888c.23-.357.606-.353.828-.008l2.887 4.482c.227.352.06.638-.357.638H6.326c-.421 0-.581-.3-.37-.648l4.006-6.622c.217-.358.567-.359.793.014l2.396 3.96 1.17-1.816zm1.59-2.735c1.14 0 2.066-.907 2.066-2.026 0-1.12-.926-2.027-2.067-2.027s-2.066.907-2.066 2.027c0 1.119.925 2.026 2.066 2.026z"> </path></svg><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr i18nString-raclU">Image</div><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr title-RrK9J">Kalanga Muya</div></div></div></figure></div></div>
<p data-aid="149807370" id="p36" style="--height:259.219px;">Fourteen-year-old Kalanga Muya said, “[Having little money,] I spent four years without attending school. … I am so grateful for what the Church has done. … I can now read, write, and speak French.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note31" data-scroll-id="note31"><sup class="marker">31</sup></a> Speaking of this initiative, the mayor of Mbuji-Mayi said, “I am inspired by The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints because while [other] churches are being divided each one in his corner … [you are working] with [others] to help the community in need.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note32" data-scroll-id="note32"><sup class="marker">32</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149807372" id="title9" style="--height:33.6111px;">Love One Another</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149807377" id="p37" style="--height:316.823px;">Each time I read <a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/nt/john/13?lang=eng">John chapter 13</a>, I am reminded of the Savior’s perfect example as a peacemaker. Jesus lovingly washed the feet of the Apostles. Then, we read, “he was troubled in spirit”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note33" data-scroll-id="note33"><sup class="marker">33</sup></a> as He thought about one He loved preparing to betray Him. I have tried to imagine the thoughts and feelings of the Savior as Judas left. Interestingly, at that sobering moment, Jesus spoke no more about His “troubling” feelings or about betrayal. Rather, He spoke to His Apostles about love, His words cascading through the centuries:</p>
<p data-aid="149807382" id="p42" style="--height:57.6042px;">“A new commandment I give unto you, That ye love one another; as I have loved you.&nbsp;…</p>
<p data-aid="149807387" id="p43" style="--height:57.6042px;">“By this shall all men know that ye are my disciples, if ye have love one to another.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/15andersen?lang=eng#note34" data-scroll-id="note34"><sup class="marker">34</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807392" id="p38" style="--height:86.4063px;">May we love Him and love one another. May we be peacemakers, that we may be called the “children of God,” I pray in the name of Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</section>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149805014" id="title2" style="--height:33.6111px;">Introduction</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149805016" id="p1" style="--height:115.208px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="21"></span>On Friday, October 28, 1588, having lost its rudder to being governed solely by oar, the ship <em>La Girona</em>, belonging to the great Spanish Armada, collided with the rocks of Lacada Point in Northern Ireland.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805018" id="p2" style="--height:115.208px;">The ship capsized. One of the castaways struggling to survive wore a gold ring given to him a few months earlier by his wife with the inscription, “I have nothing more to give you.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805020" id="p3" style="--height:86.4063px;">“I have nothing more to give you”—a phrase and a ring with the design of a hand holding a heart, an expression of love from a wife to her husband.</p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149805022" id="p4" style="--height:33.6111px;">Scripture Connection</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149805024" id="p5" style="--height:115.208px;">When I read this story, it made a deep impression on me, and I thought of the request made by the Savior: “And ye shall offer for a sacrifice unto me a broken heart and a contrite spirit.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805026" id="p6" style="--height:172.813px;">I also thought of the people’s reaction to King Benjamin’s words: “Yea, we believe all the words which thou hast spoken unto us&nbsp;…&nbsp;, which has wrought a mighty change in us, or in our hearts, that we have no more disposition to do evil, but to do good continually.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149805028" id="p8" style="--height:33.6111px;">Personal Connection</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149805030" id="p9" style="--height:57.6042px;">Let me share with you an experience I had when I was 12 years old, the effect of which lasts to this day.</p>
<p data-aid="149805032" id="p10" style="--height:57.6042px;">My mother said, “Eduardo, hurry up. We are late for the Church meetings.”</p>
<p data-aid="149805034" id="p11" style="--height:28.8021px;">“Mom, I’m going to stay with Dad today,” I replied.</p>
<p data-aid="149805037" id="p12" style="--height:57.6042px;">“Are you sure? You have to attend your priesthood quorum meeting,” she said.</p>
<p data-aid="149805040" id="p13" style="--height:57.6042px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="22"></span>I replied, “Poor Dad! He is going to be left alone. I’m going to stay with him today.”</p>
<p data-aid="149805043" id="p14" style="--height:57.6042px;">Dad was not a member of The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints.</p>
<p data-aid="149805046" id="p15" style="--height:144.01px;">My mother and sisters went to Sunday meetings. So I went to meet Dad in his workshop, where he liked to be on Sundays, and as I had told my mother, I spent a while, that is, a few minutes with him, and then I asked, “Dad, is everything all right?”</p>
<p data-aid="149805049" id="p16" style="--height:57.6042px;">He kept up his hobby of repairing radios and clocks, and he just smiled at me.</p>
<p data-aid="149805052" id="p17" style="--height:57.6042px;">Then I told him, “I’m going to go play with my friends.”</p>
<p data-aid="149805054" id="p18" style="--height:57.6042px;">Dad, without looking up, said to me, “Today is Sunday. Aren’t you supposed to go to church?”</p>
<p data-aid="149805057" id="p59" style="--height:86.4063px;">“Yes, but today I told Mom I wouldn’t go,” I replied. Dad went on about his business, and for me, that was permission to leave.</p>
<p data-aid="149805060" id="p19" style="--height:86.4063px;">That morning there was an important soccer game, and my friends had told me that I couldn’t miss it because we had to win that game.</p>
<p data-aid="149805063" id="p20" style="--height:57.6042px;">My challenge was that I had to pass in front of the chapel to get to the soccer field.</p>
<p data-aid="149805067" id="p21" style="--height:172.813px;">Determined, I dashed towards the soccer field and stopped before the great stumbling block, the chapel. I ran to the opposite sidewalk, where there were some big trees, and I decided to run between them so that no one would see me since it was the time the members were arriving at the meetings.</p>
<p data-aid="149805070" id="p22" style="--height:86.4063px;">I arrived just in time for the start of the game. I was able to play and go home before my mother got home.</p>
<p data-aid="149805074" id="p23" style="--height:115.208px;">Everything had gone well; our team had won, and I was thrilled. But that well-executed run onto the field did not go unnoticed by the deacons quorum adviser.</p>
<p data-aid="149805078" id="p24" style="--height:57.6042px;">Brother Félix Espinoza had seen me running quickly from tree to tree, trying not to be discovered.</p>
<p data-aid="149805081" id="p25" style="--height:115.208px;">At the beginning of the week, Brother Espinoza came to my house and asked to speak with me. He didn’t say anything about what he had seen on Sunday, nor did he ask me why I had missed my meeting. </p>
<p data-aid="149805085" id="p64" style="--height:172.813px;">He just handed me a manual and said, “I would like you to teach the priesthood class on Sunday. I have marked the lesson for you. It is not so difficult. I want you to read it, and I will come by in two days to help you with the preparation for the lesson.” Having said this, he handed me the manual and left.</p>
<p data-aid="149805088" id="p27" style="--height:115.208px;">I didn’t want to teach the class, but I couldn’t bring myself to tell him no. I had planned that Sunday to stay with my father again—meaning, there was another important soccer game.</p>
<p data-aid="149805091" id="p28" style="--height:86.4063px;">Brother Espinoza was a person whom young people admired.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a> He had found the restored gospel and changed his life or, in other words, his heart.</p>
<p data-aid="149805094" id="p29" style="--height:144.01px;">When Saturday afternoon arrived, I thought, “Well, maybe tomorrow I’ll wake up sick, and I won’t have to go to church.” It wasn’t the soccer game that worried me anymore; it was the class I had to teach, especially a lesson about the Sabbath day.</p>
<p data-aid="149805097" id="p30" style="--height:57.6042px;">Sunday came, and I woke up healthier than ever. I had no excuse—no escape.</p>
<p data-aid="149805100" id="p31" style="--height:86.4063px;">It was the first time I would teach a lesson, but Brother Espinoza was there by my side, and that was the day of a mighty change of heart for me.</p>
<p data-aid="149805105" id="p32" style="--height:115.208px;">From that moment on, I began to keep the Sabbath day holy, and over time, in the words of President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson, the Sabbath day has become a delight.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805108" id="p33" style="--height:57.6042px;">“Lord, I give You everything; I have nothing more to give You.”</p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149805111" id="p34" style="--height:33.6111px;">Obtaining</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149805114" id="p35" style="--height:57.6042px;">How do we obtain that mighty change of heart? It is initiated and eventually occurs</p>
<ol class="decimal" start="1">
<li data-marker="1.">
<p data-aid="149805116" id="p36" style="--height:86.4063px;">when we study the scriptures to obtain the knowledge that will strengthen our faith in Jesus Christ, which will create a desire to change;<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a></p>
</li>
<li data-marker="2.">
<p data-aid="149805118" id="p37" style="--height:57.6042px;">when we cultivate that desire through prayer and fasting;<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note8" data-scroll-id="note8"><sup class="marker">8</sup></a></p>
</li>
<li data-marker="3.">
<p data-aid="149805120" id="p38" style="--height:115.208px;">when we act, according to the word studied or received, and we make a covenant to surrender our hearts to Him, just as with King Benjamin’s people.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note9" data-scroll-id="note9"><sup class="marker">9</sup></a></p>
</li>
</ol>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149805122" id="p39" style="--height:33.6111px;">Recognition and Covenant</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149805125" id="p40" style="--height:28.8021px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="23"></span>How do we know that our heart is changing?<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note10" data-scroll-id="note10"><sup class="marker">10</sup></a></p>
<ol class="decimal" start="1">
<li data-marker="1.">
<p data-aid="149805127" id="p41" style="--height:28.8021px;">When we want to please God in all things.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note11" data-scroll-id="note11"><sup class="marker">11</sup></a></p>
</li>
<li data-marker="2.">
<p data-aid="149805128" id="p42" style="--height:57.6042px;">When we treat others with love, respect, and consideration.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note12" data-scroll-id="note12"><sup class="marker">12</sup></a></p>
</li>
<li data-marker="3.">
<p data-aid="149805130" id="p43" style="--height:57.6042px;">When we see that the attributes of Christ are becoming part of our character.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note13" data-scroll-id="note13"><sup class="marker">13</sup></a></p>
</li>
<li data-marker="4.">
<p data-aid="149805133" id="p44" style="--height:57.6042px;">When we feel the guidance of the Holy Spirit more constantly.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note14" data-scroll-id="note14"><sup class="marker">14</sup></a></p>
</li>
<li data-marker="5.">
<p data-aid="149805136" id="p45" style="--height:86.4063px;">When we keep a commandment that has been difficult for us to obey and then continue to live it.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note15" data-scroll-id="note15"><sup class="marker">15</sup></a></p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-aid="149805137" id="p46" style="--height:86.4063px;">When we listen carefully to our leaders’ advice and cheerfully decide to follow it, have we not experienced a mighty change of heart?</p>
<p data-aid="149805139" id="p47" style="--height:57.6042px;">“Lord, I give You everything; I have nothing more to give You.”</p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149805141" id="p48" style="--height:33.6111px;">Maintenance and Benefits</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149805143" id="p49" style="--height:28.8021px;">How do we maintain the mighty change?</p>
<ol class="decimal" start="1">
<li data-marker="1.">
<p data-aid="149805145" id="p60" style="--height:115.208px;">When we partake of the sacrament weekly and renew the covenant to take upon us the name of Christ, always remember Him, and keep His commandments.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note16" data-scroll-id="note16"><sup class="marker">16</sup></a></p>
</li>
<li data-marker="2.">
<p data-aid="149805147" id="p61" style="--height:115.208px;">When we turn our lives toward the temple.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note17" data-scroll-id="note17"><sup class="marker">17</sup></a> Regular temple attendance will help us maintain a new and renewed heart as we participate in the ordinances.</p>
</li>
<li data-marker="3.">
<p data-aid="149805149" id="p62" style="--height:57.6042px;">When we love and serve our neighbors by ministering activities and missionary work.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note18" data-scroll-id="note18"><sup class="marker">18</sup></a></p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-aid="149805151" id="p50" style="--height:86.4063px;">Then for our great joy, that inner change is strengthened and spreads until it abounds in good works.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note19" data-scroll-id="note19"><sup class="marker">19</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805152" id="p51" style="--height:57.6042px;">This mighty change of heart brings us a feeling of freedom, trust, and peace.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note20" data-scroll-id="note20"><sup class="marker">20</sup></a></p>
