<p data-aid="149805154" id="p52" style="--height:144.01px;">This change of heart is not an event; it takes faith, repentance, and constant spiritual work to happen. It begins when we desire to submit our will to the Lord, and it materializes when we enter into and keep covenants with Him.</p>
<p data-aid="149805157" id="p53" style="--height:57.6042px;">That individual action has a positive effect both on us and on the people around us.</p>
<p data-aid="149805160" id="p54" style="--height:201.615px;">In the words of President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson, “Imagine how quickly the devastating conflicts throughout the world—and those in our individual lives—would be resolved if we all chose to follow Jesus Christ and heed His teachings.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note21" data-scroll-id="note21"><sup class="marker">21</sup></a> This action of following the Savior’s teachings leads to a mighty change of heart.</p>
<p data-aid="149805164" id="p63" style="--height:144.01px;">Dear brothers and sisters, young people, and children, as we participate in the conference this weekend, let the words of our prophets, which will come from the Lord, enter our hearts to experience a mighty change.</p>
<p data-aid="149805168" id="p56" style="--height:144.01px;">For those who have not yet joined the Lord’s restored Church, I invite you to listen to the missionaries with a sincere desire to know what God expects of you and experience that inner transformation.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note22" data-scroll-id="note22"><sup class="marker">22</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805172" id="p57" style="--height:86.4063px;">Today is the day to decide to follow the Lord Jesus Christ. “Lord, I give You my heart; I have nothing more to give You.”</p>
<p data-aid="149805176" id="p58" style="--height:201.615px;">Just as the ring was recovered from that shipwreck, when we give our hearts to God, we are rescued from the raging seas of this life, and in the process we are refined and purified through the Atonement of Christ and become “children of Christ,” being spiritually “born of Him.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/16gavarret?lang=eng#note23" data-scroll-id="note23"><sup class="marker">23</sup></a> Of this I testify in the name of Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</section>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149807228" id="p1" style="--height:86.4063px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="24"></span>How will life’s challenges affect our faith in Jesus Christ? And what effect will our faith have on the joy and peace we experience in this life?</p>
<p data-aid="149807232" id="p2" style="--height:288.021px;">The year was 1977. The phone rang, and the message tore our hearts apart. Carolyn and Doug Tebbs were in the process of moving to their new home after completing graduate school. The elders quorum had come to load the moving van. Doug, making sure the path was clear before backing out, took one last look. What he could not see was his little daughter, Jennie, dart behind the truck at just the wrong moment. In an instant, their beloved Jennie was gone.</p>
<p data-aid="149807235" id="p3" style="--height:144.01px;">What would happen next? Would the pain they so deeply felt and the inconceivable sense of loss create an irreconcilable chasm between Carolyn and Doug, or would it somehow bind their hearts together and solidify their faith in Heavenly Father’s plan?</p>
<p data-aid="149807237" id="p4" style="--height:201.615px;">The road through their afflictions has been long and painful, but from somewhere came the spiritual reserves to not lose hope but to “hold on [their] way.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a> Somehow this incredible couple became even more Christlike. More committed. More compassionate. They believed that, in His time, God would consecrate their afflictions for their gain.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807241" id="p5" style="--height:144.01px;">Though the pain and loss would not and could not leave completely, Carolyn and Doug have been comforted by the assurance that by their staying firmly on the covenant path, their beloved Jennie would be theirs forever.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807244" id="p6" style="--height:172.813px;">Their example has strengthened my faith in the Lord’s plan. We don’t see all things. He does. The Lord told Joseph Smith in Liberty Jail that “all these things shall give thee experience, and shall be for thy good. The Son of Man hath descended below them all. Art thou greater than he?”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807247" id="p7" style="--height:259.219px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="25"></span>As we accept the Lord’s will, He teaches us how to walk with Him.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a> As a young missionary serving in Tahiti, I was asked to administer to a sick infant. We laid our hands on his head and blessed him to get better. His health began to improve, but then he fell sick again. A second time we blessed him but with the same result. A third request came. We pleaded with the Lord that His will be done. Shortly after, this little spirit returned to his heavenly home.</p>
<p data-aid="149807251" id="p8" style="--height:115.208px;">But we were at peace. We wanted the infant to live, but the Lord had other plans. Accepting His will in place of our own is key to finding joy no matter our circumstances.</p>
<p data-aid="149807254" id="p9" style="--height:230.417px;">The simple faith we have in Jesus Christ as we first begin to learn about Him can remain in our hearts as we confront life’s challenges. Our faith in Him can and will guide us through the complexities of life. Indeed, we will find that there is simplicity on the other side of life’s complexities<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a> as we remain “[steadfast] in Christ, having a perfect brightness of hope.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807256" id="p10" style="--height:144.01px;">Part of life’s purpose is to allow these potential stumbling blocks to become stepping-stones as we climb what I call the “ladder of faith”—a ladder because it suggests that faith is not static. It can go up or down according to the choices we make.</p>
<p data-aid="149807260" id="p11" style="--height:172.813px;">As we strive to build faith in the Savior, we may not fully comprehend God’s love for us, and we may obey His laws out of a sense of obligation. Guilt may even become our primary motivator rather than love. A real connection to Him may not yet have been experienced.</p>
<p data-aid="149807263" id="p12" style="--height:172.813px;">As we seek to increase our faith, we may be confused by what James taught. He reminded us that “faith without works is dead.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note8" data-scroll-id="note8"><sup class="marker">8</sup></a> We may stumble if we think everything depends on us. An overdependence on ourselves can impede our ability to access the powers of heaven.</p>
<p data-aid="149807267" id="p13" style="--height:288.021px;">But as we move toward true faith in Jesus Christ, our mindset begins to change. We recognize that obedience and faith in the Savior qualify us to have His Spirit always to be with us.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note9" data-scroll-id="note9"><sup class="marker">9</sup></a> Obedience is no longer an irritant but becomes a quest.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note10" data-scroll-id="note10"><sup class="marker">10</sup></a> We recognize that obedience to God’s commands enables us to be trusted of Him. With His trust comes increased light. This light guides our journey and allows us to see more clearly the path we should take.</p>
<p data-aid="149807271" id="p14" style="--height:201.615px;">But there is more. As our faith in the Savior increases, we observe a subtle shift that includes a divine understanding of our relationship with God—a steady movement away from “What do I want?” to “What does God want?” Like the Savior, we want to act “not as I will, but as thou wilt.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note11" data-scroll-id="note11"><sup class="marker">11</sup></a> We want to do God’s work and be an instrument in His hands.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note12" data-scroll-id="note12"><sup class="marker">12</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807275" id="p15" style="--height:230.417px;">Our progression is an eternal one. President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson has taught that there is so much more that Heavenly Father wants us to know.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note13" data-scroll-id="note13"><sup class="marker">13</sup></a> As we progress, we better understand what the Lord taught Joseph Smith: “For if you keep my commandments you shall receive of his fulness, and be glorified in me; … I say unto you, you shall receive grace for grace.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note14" data-scroll-id="note14"><sup class="marker">14</sup></a> </p>
<p data-aid="149807280" id="p16" style="--height:144.01px;">How high we climb on the ladder of faith is our decision. Elder Neil&nbsp;L. Andersen taught that “faith is not by chance, but by choice.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note15" data-scroll-id="note15"><sup class="marker">15</sup></a> We can choose to make the choices needed to increase our faith in the Savior.</p>
<p data-aid="149807284" id="p17" style="--height:201.615px;">Consider the impact of the choices made when Laman and Lemuel descended the ladder of faith while Nephi climbed higher. Is there a clearer representation than the difference between Nephi’s response of “I will go and do”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note16" data-scroll-id="note16"><sup class="marker">16</sup></a> versus Laman and Lemuel, having just seen an angel, <span class="page-break" data-page="26"></span>responding with “How is it possible that the Lord will deliver?”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note17" data-scroll-id="note17"><sup class="marker">17</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807288" id="p18" style="--height:86.4063px;">Unbelief blocks our ability to see miracles, whereas a mindset of faith in the Savior unlocks the powers of heaven.</p>
<p data-aid="149807292" id="p19" style="--height:201.615px;">Even when our faith is weak, the Lord’s hand will always be stretched out.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note18" data-scroll-id="note18"><sup class="marker">18</sup></a> Years ago I received the assignment to reorganize a stake in Nigeria. At the last minute, there was a change in the date. There was a man in the stake who had decided to skip town for the first conference date. He did not want to risk being called as the stake president.</p>
<p data-aid="149807296" id="p20" style="--height:172.813px;">While he was away, he was in a terrible accident, but he was unharmed. This caused him to consider why his life had been spared. He revisited the decision he had made. He repented and humbly attended the new conference date. And yes, he was called to be the new stake president.</p>
<p data-aid="149807300" id="p21" style="--height:86.4063px;">Elder Neal&nbsp;A. Maxwell taught: “Only by aligning our wills with God’s is full happiness to be found. Anything less results in a lesser portion.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note19" data-scroll-id="note19"><sup class="marker">19</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807304" id="p22" style="--height:230.417px;">After doing “all things that lie in our power,” then it is time to “stand still … to see the salvation of God.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note20" data-scroll-id="note20"><sup class="marker">20</sup></a> I saw this while serving as a ministering brother to the McCormick family. Married for 21 years, Mary Kay served faithfully in her callings. Ken was not a member of the Church and had no interest in becoming one, but loving his wife, he chose to attend church with her.</p>
<p data-aid="149807311" id="p23" style="--height:86.4063px;">One Sunday I felt impressed to share my testimony with Ken. I asked him if I could do so. His response was simple and clear: “No, thank you.”</p>
<p data-aid="149807318" id="p24" style="--height:144.01px;">I was puzzled. I had felt a prompting and tried to follow it. It was tempting to decide that I had done my part. But after prayer and reflection, I could see that though my intentions were correct, I had relied too much on myself and too little on the Lord.</p>
<p data-aid="149807320" id="p25" style="--height:144.01px;">Later I returned but with a different mindset. I would go simply as an instrument in the Lord’s hands, with no other desire than to follow the Spirit. Together with my faithful companion, Gerald Cardon, we entered the McCormick home.</p>
<p data-aid="149807326" id="p26" style="--height:230.417px;">Soon after, I felt prompted to invite Gerald to sing “I Know That My Redeemer Lives.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note21" data-scroll-id="note21"><sup class="marker">21</sup></a> He gave me a questioning look, but having faith in my faith, he did it. A beautiful spirit filled the room. The prompting came to invite Mary Kay and Kristin, their daughter, to share their testimonies. As they did so, the Spirit grew stronger. In fact, after Kristin’s testimony, tears were streaming down Ken’s cheeks.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note22" data-scroll-id="note22"><sup class="marker">22</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807332" id="p27" style="--height:172.813px;">God had taken over. Hearts were not just touched but changed forever. Twenty-one years of unbelief were washed away by the power of the Holy Ghost. A week later, Ken was baptized. A year later, Ken and Mary Kay were sealed in the house of the Lord for time and for all eternity.</p>
<p data-aid="149807336" id="p28" style="--height:86.4063px;">Together we had experienced what it meant to replace our will with the Lord’s will, and our faith in Him increased.</p>
<p data-aid="149807340" id="p29" style="--height:57.6042px;">Please consider a few questions posed by God’s prophets as you strive to climb your ladder of faith:</p>
<p data-aid="149807345" id="p30" style="--height:28.8021px;">Am I stripped of pride?<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note23" data-scroll-id="note23"><sup class="marker">23</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807352" id="p31" style="--height:28.8021px;">Do I give place in my heart for the word of God?<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note24" data-scroll-id="note24"><sup class="marker">24</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807356" id="p32" style="--height:57.6042px;">Do I allow my afflictions to be consecrated for my gain?<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note25" data-scroll-id="note25"><sup class="marker">25</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807361" id="p33" style="--height:57.6042px;">Am I willing to let my will be swallowed up in the will of the Father?<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note26" data-scroll-id="note26"><sup class="marker">26</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807364" id="p34" style="--height:57.6042px;">If I have felt to sing the song of redeeming love, can I feel so now?<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note27" data-scroll-id="note27"><sup class="marker">27</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807369" id="p35" style="--height:28.8021px;">Do I let God prevail in my life?<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/17kacher?lang=eng#note28" data-scroll-id="note28"><sup class="marker">28</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807371" id="p36" style="--height:115.208px;">If you find your current path in conflict with your faith in the Savior, then please find your way back to Him. Your exaltation and that of your posterity depend on it.</p>
<p data-aid="149807376" id="p37" style="--height:115.208px;">May we plant the seeds of faith deep in our hearts. May we nourish these seeds as we bind ourselves to the Savior by honoring the covenants we have made with Him. In the name of Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149805050" id="p1" style="--height:172.813px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="27"></span>My dear brothers and sisters, we have been blessed today to hear inspired servants of God give counsel and encouragement. Each of us, wherever we are, knows that we live in increasingly perilous times. My prayer is that I might help you stand steady in the storms we face, with a peaceful heart.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/18eyring?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805055" id="p2" style="--height:172.813px;">The place to begin is to remember that we are each a beloved child of God and that He has inspired servants. Those servants of God have foreseen the times in which we live. The Apostle Paul wrote to Timothy, “This know also, that in the last days perilous times shall come.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/18eyring?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805058" id="p3" style="--height:201.615px;">Anyone with eyes to see the signs of the times and ears to hear the words of prophets knows that is true. The perils of greatest danger come to us from the forces of wickedness. Those forces are increasing. And so it will become more difficult, not easier, to honor the covenants we must make and keep to live the gospel of Jesus Christ.</p>
<p data-aid="149805061" id="p4" style="--height:86.4063px;">For those of us who are concerned for ourselves and for those we love, <span class="page-break" data-page="28"></span>there is hope in the promise God has made of a place of safety in the storms ahead.</p>
<p data-aid="149805065" id="p5" style="--height:460.833px;">Here is a word picture of that place. It has been repeatedly described by living prophets. For example, as recorded in the Book of Mormon, an inspired and loving father told his sons how to strengthen themselves to stand steady in the storms ahead of them: “And now, my sons, remember, remember that it is upon the rock of our Redeemer, who is Christ, the Son of God, that ye must build your foundation; that when the devil shall send forth his mighty winds, yea, his shafts in the whirlwind, yea, when all his hail and his mighty storm shall beat upon you, it shall have no power over you to drag you down to the gulf of misery and endless wo, because of the rock upon which ye are built, which is a sure foundation, … whereon if men build they cannot fall.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/18eyring?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805068" id="p7" style="--height:230.417px;">The misery and endless woe of which he spoke are the terrible effects of sins should we not fully repent of them. The growing storms are the temptations and the increasing attacks of Satan. It has never been more important than it is now to understand how to build on that sure foundation. For me, there is no better place to look than in the last sermon of King Benjamin, also recorded in the Book of Mormon.</p>
<p data-aid="149805071" id="p8" style="--height:172.813px;">King Benjamin’s prophetic words are applicable to us in our day. He knew from his own experience the terrors of war. He had defended his people in combat, relying on the power of God. He saw clearly the terrible powers of Lucifer to tempt, to try to overcome, and to discourage God’s children.</p>
<p data-aid="149805073" id="p9" style="--height:201.615px;">He invited his people and us to build on the only sure rock of safety, who is the Savior. He made clear that we are free to choose between right and wrong and that we cannot avoid the consequences of our choices. He spoke directly and sharply because he knew what sorrow would come to those who might not hear and heed his warnings.</p>
<p data-aid="149805077" id="p10" style="--height:115.208px;">Here is how he described the consequences that follow our choice either to follow the prompting of the Spirit or to follow the evil messages that come from Satan, whose intent is to tempt and destroy us:</p>
<p data-aid="149805080" id="p11" style="--height:201.615px;">“For behold, there is a wo pronounced upon him who listeth to obey that [evil] spirit; for if he listeth to obey him, and remaineth and dieth in his sins, the same drinketh damnation to his own soul; for he receiveth for his wages an everlasting punishment, having transgressed the law of God contrary to his own knowledge.&nbsp;…</p>
<p data-aid="149805084" id="p12" style="--height:230.417px;">“Therefore if that man repenteth not, and remaineth and dieth an enemy to God, the demands of divine justice do awaken his immortal soul to a lively sense of his own guilt, which doth cause him to shrink from the presence of the Lord, and doth fill his breast with guilt, and pain, and anguish, which is like an unquenchable fire, whose flame ascendeth up forever and ever.”</p>
<p data-aid="149805087" id="p13" style="--height:201.615px;">King Benjamin went on to say, “O, all ye old men, and also ye young men, and you little children who can understand my words, for I have spoken plainly unto you that ye might understand, I pray that ye should awake to a remembrance of the awful situation of those that have fallen into transgression.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/18eyring?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805090" id="p14" style="--height:172.813px;">For me, the power of that warning to repent forms in my mind a picture of the sure time when you and I will stand before the Savior after this life. We want with all our hearts not to shrink but rather to look up at Him, see Him smile, and hear Him say, “Well done, thou good and faithful servant: … enter [in].”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/18eyring?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805093" id="p15" style="--height:316.823px;">King Benjamin makes it clear how we can receive the hope to hear those words if we find the way in this life to have our natures changed through the Atonement of Jesus Christ. That is the only way we can build on the sure foundation and so stand firm during the storms of temptations and trials ahead. King Benjamin describes that change in our natures with a beautiful metaphor that has always touched my heart. It <span class="page-break" data-page="29"></span>was used by prophets for millennia and by the Lord Himself. It is this: we must become as a child—a little child.</p>
<p data-aid="149805096" id="p16" style="--height:374.427px;">For some, that will not be easy to accept. Most of us want to be strong. We may well see being like a child as being weak. Most parents look for the day when their children act less childish. But King Benjamin, who understood as well as any mortal what it meant to be a man of strength and courage, makes it clear that to be like a child is not to be childish. It is to be like the Savior, who prayed to His Father for strength to be able to do His Father’s will and atone for the sins of all of His Father’s children and then did it. Our natures must be changed to become as a child to gain the strength we must have to stand steady and at peace in times of peril.</p>
<p data-aid="149805099" id="p17" style="--height:316.823px;">Here is King Benjamin’s stirring description of how that change comes: “For the natural man is an enemy to God, and has been from the fall of Adam, and will be, forever and ever, unless he yields to the enticings of the Holy Spirit, and putteth off the natural man and becometh a saint through the atonement of Christ the Lord, and becometh as a child, submissive, meek, humble, patient, full of love, willing to submit to all things which the Lord seeth fit to inflict upon him, even as a child doth submit to his father.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/18eyring?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805102" id="p18" style="--height:201.615px;">We receive that change as we make and renew covenants with God. That brings the power of Christ’s Atonement to allow a transformation in our hearts. We can feel it every time we partake of the sacrament, perform a temple ordinance for a departed ancestor, testify as a witness of the Savior, or care for someone in need as Christ’s disciple.</p>
<p data-aid="149805104" id="p19" style="--height:201.615px;">In those experiences, we become over time like a child in our capacity to love and obey. We come to stand on the sure foundation. Our faith in Jesus Christ brings us to repentance and to keeping His commandments. We obey, and we gain power to resist temptation, and we gain the promised companionship of the Holy Ghost.</p>
<p data-aid="149805107" id="p20" style="--height:144.01px;">Our natures change to become as a little child, obedient to God and more loving. That change will qualify us to enjoy the gifts that come through the Holy Ghost. Having the Spirit’s companionship will comfort, guide, and strengthen us.</p>
<p data-aid="149805110" id="p21" style="--height:230.417px;">I have come to know some of what King Benjamin meant when he said that we could become like a little child before God. I have learned from many experiences that the Holy Ghost speaks most often in a quiet voice, heard most easily when one’s heart is meek and submissive, like that of a child. In fact, the prayer that works is “I want only what You want. Just tell me what that is. I’ll do it.”</p>
<p data-aid="149805113" id="p22" style="--height:201.615px;">When the storms in life come, you can be steady because you are standing on the rock of your faith in Jesus Christ. That faith will lead you to daily repentance and consistent covenant keeping. Then you will always remember Him. And through the storms of hatred and wickedness, you will feel steady and hopeful.</p>
<p data-aid="149805115" id="p23" style="--height:144.01px;">More than that, you will find yourself reaching out to lift others to safety on the rock with you. Faith in Jesus Christ always leads to greater hope and to feelings of charity toward others, which is the true love of Christ.</p>
<p data-aid="149805117" id="p24" style="--height:201.615px;">I bear you my solemn witness that the Lord Jesus Christ has given you the invitation “Come unto me.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/18eyring?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a> He invites you, out of love for you and for those you love, to come to Him for peace in this life and eternal life in the world to come. He knows perfectly the storms you will face in your test as part of the plan of happiness.</p>
<p data-aid="149805119" id="p25" style="--height:230.417px;">I plead with you to accept the Savior’s invitation. Like a meek and loving child, accept His help. Make and keep the covenants He offers in The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints. They will strengthen you. The Savior knows the storms and the places of safety on the way home to Him and to our Heavenly Father. He knows the way. He is the Way. I so testify in the sacred name of Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149807347" id="p1" style="--height:115.208px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="34"></span>I direct my remarks today to the young people of the Church, meaning anyone President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson’s age or younger. I seldom use visuals, but I can’t resist sharing this one.</p>
<div><div class="imageWrapper-wTPPD"><img id="img1" data-img-id="407ff444b12011ec8edaeeeeac1ec8604842ceec" data-assetid="407ff444b12011ec8edaeeeeac1ec8604842ceec" data-missing-asset="false" data-width="500" data-height="323" data-aspect-ratio="1.5479876160990713" alt="Child's Note" class="imageWithModal-bCN6D" height="323" src="https://assets.ldscdn.org/ea/97/ea97a780d75c1a1b2ec8cfc8fd38574da6dce5c2/holland_child_note_bishop.png" srcset="https://assets.ldscdn.org/e5/79/e5790bdf5e45b0e271b50a50b88bb50e3f9d6a43/holland_child_note_bishop.png 60w,https://assets.ldscdn.org/df/d9/dfd9157c5b7c2c5d60f6a90f81cbba3f8a98887d/holland_child_note_bishop.png 100w,https://assets.ldscdn.org/df/9d/df9d8b36f39382cdc34fadc4fc2eae056232512c/holland_child_note_bishop.png 200w,https://assets.ldscdn.org/70/d3/70d3812c01ccc8f5f960c64e5a4d6aee3b67e2eb/holland_child_note_bishop.png 250w,https://assets.ldscdn.org/11/61/11616fb7c15d326a70872df110722362a1f52dde/holland_child_note_bishop.png 320w,https://assets.ldscdn.org/ea/97/ea97a780d75c1a1b2ec8cfc8fd38574da6dce5c2/holland_child_note_bishop.png 500w,https://assets.ldscdn.org/35/f4/35f4da4557da390260699793edc746539761e9a8/holland_child_note_bishop.png 640w" width="500"></div></div>
<p data-aid="149807353" id="p2" style="--height:86.4063px;">This <em>cri de coeur</em> comes from my eight-year-old friend Marin Arnold, written when she was seven. I will translate for you her early reformed Egyptian:</p>
<div class="poetry">
<div class="stanza">
<p class="line" data-aid="149807358" id="p3" style="--height:28.8021px;">Dear Bishop</p>
<p class="line" data-aid="149807363" id="p4" style="--height:28.8021px;">generle confrins</p>
<p class="line" data-aid="149807367" id="p5" style="--height:28.8021px;">was Boring why</p>
<p class="line" data-aid="149807374" id="p6" style="--height:28.8021px;">Do we half to</p>
<p class="line" data-aid="149807380" id="p7" style="--height:28.8021px;">Do it? tell me why</p>
<p class="line" data-aid="149807384" id="p8" style="--height:28.8021px;">Sinserlie, Marin</p>
<p class="line" data-aid="149807390" id="p9" style="--height:28.8021px;">Arnold.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a></p>
</div>
</div>
<p data-aid="149807397" id="p10" style="--height:144.01px;">Well, Marin, the talk I am about to give will undoubtedly disappoint you again. But when you write your bishop to complain, it is important that you tell him my name is “Kearon. Elder Patrick Kearon.”</p>
<p data-aid="149807403" id="p11" style="--height:288.021px;">For nearly two years a pandemic of biblical proportions has enveloped our planet, and while that plague brought a halt to almost everything socially, obviously it did not bring a halt to brutality, violence, and cruel aggression politically—nationally or internationally. As if that were not enough, we are still facing long-standing social and cultural challenges, ranging from economic deprivation to environmental desecration to racial inequity and more.</p>
<p data-aid="149807409" id="p22" style="--height:259.219px;">Such stiff winds and dark days can be discouraging to the youth among us, those to whom we look for optimism and enthusiasm regarding the tomorrows of our lives. It has been said that “the power of youth is the common wealth for the entire world. The … young … are the faces of our … future.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a> Furthermore, our children are the trustees into whose hands the destiny of this Church will be placed.</p>
<p data-aid="149807415" id="p12" style="--height:345.625px;">Given our current times, it is understandable if the idealism of the young is waning a little. Dr. Laurie Santos, a professor at Yale University, recently created a class titled Psychology and the Good Life. “The first year the class was offered, nearly [one-quarter] of the <em>[entire]</em> undergraduate student body enrolled.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a> Over 64 million people then visited her podcast. Writing about this phenomenon, one journalist noted how painful it is to see so many bright, young students—and adults—desperately “looking for something they’ve lost” or, worse yet, longing for something they never had.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807421" id="p13" style="--height:345.625px;">My plea today to our youth, and to you parents and adults who advise them, is to begin your search for happiness by embracing the bounty we have already received from the giver of every good gift.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a> At precisely the moment many in the world are asking deep questions of the soul, <span class="page-break" data-page="35"></span>we ought to be answering with the “good news”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a> of the gospel of Jesus Christ. The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints, which holds aloft the mission and message of the Savior of the world, offers the most eternally significant way to both find good and do good at such a needful time.</p>
<p data-aid="149807427" id="p23" style="--height:259.219px;">President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson has said that this generation of young people has the capacity to have “more impact [for good] on the world than any previous generation.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a> We, of all people, should be “sing[ing] the song of redeeming love,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note8" data-scroll-id="note8"><sup class="marker">8</sup></a> but that takes discipline—“discipleship,” if you will—the kind that guards against negative attitudes and destructive habits that would pull us off-key as we try to sing that song of eternal salvation.</p>
<p data-aid="149807433" id="p14" style="--height:432.031px;">Even as we stay “on the sunny side of the street,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note9" data-scroll-id="note9"><sup class="marker">9</sup></a> we do run into that fellow from time to time who is determined to find something bleak and dismal about everything. You know his motto: “It is always darkest just before it goes pitch-black.” What a malignant vision, and what a miserable existence! Yes, we might sometimes want to run away from where we are, but we certainly should never run away from who we are—children of the living God who loves us, who is always ready to forgive us, and who will never, ever forsake us. You are His most precious possession. You are His child, to whom He has given prophets and promises, spiritual gifts and revelations, miracles and messages, and angels on both sides of the veil.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note10" data-scroll-id="note10"><sup class="marker">10</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807439" id="p24" style="--height:518.438px;">He has also given you a church that strengthens families for mortality and binds them together for eternity. It provides more than 31,000 wards and branches where people gather and sing and fast and pray for each other and give of their means to the poor. This is where every person is named, accounted for, and ministered to and where lay friends and neighbors voluntarily serve each other in callings that range from clerical work to custodial duty. Young adults—and senior couples as well—serve missions by the thousands at their own expense with no say whatsoever as to where they will labor, and members young and old trundle off to temples to perform sacred ordinances necessary to bind the human family together—a bold activity in such a divided world but one which declares that such divisiveness is only temporary. These are a few of the reasons we give for “the hope that is in [us].”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note11" data-scroll-id="note11"><sup class="marker">11</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807445" id="p15" style="--height:374.427px;">Of course, in our present day, tremendously difficult issues face any disciple of Jesus Christ. The leaders of this Church are giving their lives to seeking the Lord’s guidance in the resolution of these challenges. If some are <em>not</em> resolved to the satisfaction of everyone, perhaps they constitute part of the cross Jesus said we would have to take up in order to follow Him.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note12" data-scroll-id="note12"><sup class="marker">12</sup></a> It is precisely because there would be dark days and difficult issues that God promised He would, out of a cloud by day and a pillar of fire by night, guide prophets, give an iron rod, open a narrow gate leading to a strait path, and above all grant us the power to finish the course.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note13" data-scroll-id="note13"><sup class="marker">13</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807452" id="p16" style="--height:144.01px;">So please, please, stay for the whole feast even if you are not sure about the broccoli. Bask in <em>His</em> light and lend <em>your</em> candle to the cause.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note14" data-scroll-id="note14"><sup class="marker">14</sup></a> They have it right in Primary: Jesus really <em>does</em> “[want you] for a sunbeam.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note15" data-scroll-id="note15"><sup class="marker">15</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807457" id="p17" style="--height:144.01px;">When the Jewish leader Jairus pled for Jesus to heal his 12-year-old daughter, who lay dying at home, the surrounding crowd waylaid the Savior so long that a servant soon came saying to this anxious father, “Thy daughter is dead; trouble not the Master.”</p>
<p data-aid="149807463" id="p18" style="--height:86.4063px;">“But when Jesus heard it, he answered him, saying, Fear not: believe only, and she shall be made whole.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note16" data-scroll-id="note16"><sup class="marker">16</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807469" id="p21" style="--height:57.6042px;">And she was. And so will you. “Fear not: believe only.”</p>
<p data-aid="149807473" id="p19" style="--height:403.229px;">Because each of you in this audience is precious to God and to this Church, I close with this special apostolic declaration. Before you ever <span class="page-break" data-page="36"></span>received the gift of the Holy Ghost, you had the Light of Christ planted in your soul,<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note17" data-scroll-id="note17"><sup class="marker">17</sup></a> that “light which is in all things, … giveth life to all things,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note18" data-scroll-id="note18"><sup class="marker">18</sup></a> and is the influence for good in the hearts of all people who have ever lived or ever will live. That light was given to protect you and teach you. One of its central messages is that life is the most precious of all gifts, a gift which is obtained eternally only through the Atonement of the Lord Jesus Christ. As the Light and Life of the World,<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note19" data-scroll-id="note19"><sup class="marker">19</sup></a> the Only Begotten Son of God came to give us life by conquering death.</p>
<p data-aid="149807479" id="p25" style="--height:172.813px;">We must commit ourselves fully to that gift of life and run to the aid of those who are at risk of giving up this sacred gift. Leaders, advisers, friends, family—watch for signs of depression, despair, or anything hinting of self-harm. Offer your help. Listen. Make some kind of intervention as appropriate.</p>
<p data-aid="149807486" id="p26" style="--height:403.229px;">To any of our youth out there who are struggling, whatever your concerns or difficulties, death by suicide is manifestly <em>not</em> the answer. It will not relieve the pain you are feeling or that you think you are causing. In a world that so desperately needs all the light it can get, please do <em>not</em> minimize the eternal light God put in <em>your</em> soul before this world was. Talk to someone. Ask for help. Do <em>not</em> destroy a life that Christ gave <em>His</em> life to preserve. You can bear the struggles of this mortal life because we will help you bear them. You are stronger than you think. Help <em>is</em> available, from others and especially from God. You are loved and valued and needed. We need you! “Fear not: believe only.”</p>
<p data-aid="149807492" id="p20" style="--height:259.219px;">Someone who faced circumstances far more desperate than you and I ever will once cried: “Go forward [my beloved young friends]. Courage, … and on, on to the victory! Let your hearts rejoice, and be exceedingly glad.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/23holland?lang=eng#note20" data-scroll-id="note20"><sup class="marker">20</sup></a> We have so much to be glad about. We have each other, and we have Him. Don’t deny us the chance to have you, I plead, in the sacred and holy name of the Lord Jesus Christ, our Master, amen.</p>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149805148" id="p47" style="--height:57.6042px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="37"></span>Marin, I’m Elder Holland, and things are about to go downhill.</p>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149805150" id="title2" style="--height:33.6111px;">We Are More Than Conquerors</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149805153" id="p1" style="--height:144.01px;">We are all intrigued by survival stories. We hear tales of intrepid explorers and ordinary people alike who manage to keep themselves alive against all odds and expectations, and we can’t help but ask ourselves, “Could I have done that?”</p>
<p data-aid="149805156" id="p2" style="--height:201.615px;">I think immediately of British explorer Ernest Shackleton and the crew of his ship HMS <i>Endurance</i>, shipwrecked in Antarctic ice and then stranded on a barren island for nearly two years. Shackleton’s extraordinary leadership and indomitable resolve saved the lives of his men, despite the harshest conditions.</p>
<p data-aid="149805159" id="p45" style="--height:172.813px;">Then I think of the crew of Apollo 13 hurtling through space to land on the moon! But disaster struck when an oxygen tank exploded, and the mission had to be aborted. Short of oxygen, the crew and mission control ingeniously improvised and brought all three astronauts safely back to earth.</p>
<p data-aid="149805163" id="p3" style="--height:201.615px;">I marvel at the astonishing survival of individuals and families victimized by war, imprisoned in camps, and those who become refugees who heroically and courageously keep alive the flame of hope for fellow sufferers, who impart goodness in the face of brutality, and who somehow manage to help others endure just one more day.</p>
<p data-aid="149805167" id="p4" style="--height:57.6042px;">Could you or I survive in any one of these extreme circumstances?</p>
<p data-aid="149805171" id="p5" style="--height:259.219px;">Perhaps some of you, however, consider the accounts of survivors, and your soul cries out that <em>you are</em> living a survival story <em>right now</em> as a victim of abuse, neglect, bullying, domestic violence, or any suffering of this kind. You are in the midst of your own desperate attempt to survive a situation that feels very much like a disastrous shipwreck or a promising mission suddenly aborted. Will you ever be rescued; will you make it through your own survival story?</p>
<p data-aid="149805174" id="p6" style="--height:259.219px;">The answer is <em>yes</em>. You can survive. You have in fact already been rescued; you have already been saved—by the One who has suffered the very torment you are suffering and endured the very agony you are enduring.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a> Jesus has overcome the abuses of this world<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a> to give you power to not only <em>survive</em> but one day, through Him, to overcome and even <em>conquer</em>—to completely rise above the pain, the misery, the anguish, and see them replaced by peace.</p>
<p data-aid="149805178" id="p7" style="--height:28.8021px;">The Apostle Paul asks:</p>
<p data-aid="149805183" id="p36" style="--height:86.4063px;">“Who shall separate us from the love of Christ? shall tribulation, or distress, or persecution, or famine, or nakedness, or peril, or sword?&nbsp;…</p>
<p data-aid="149805187" id="p37" style="--height:57.6042px;">“Nay, in <em>all</em> these things we are <em>more than conquerors through him that loved us</em>.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149805192" id="title3" style="--height:33.6111px;">The Promises to Covenant Israel</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149805198" id="p8" style="--height:172.813px;">You will remember when President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson issued the following invitation in general conference. He said: “As you study your scriptures&nbsp;…&nbsp;, I encourage you to make a <span class="page-break" data-page="38"></span>list of all that the Lord has promised He will do for covenant Israel. I think you will be astounded!”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805203" id="p9" style="--height:115.208px;">Here are just a few of the powerful and comforting promises our family found. Imagine the Lord speaking these words to you—to <em>you</em> who are surviving—because they <em>are</em> for you:</p>
<p data-aid="149805209" id="p10" style="--height:28.8021px;">Fear not.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805219" id="p38" style="--height:57.6042px;">I know your sorrows, and I have come to deliver you.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805225" id="p39" style="--height:28.8021px;">I will not leave you.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805232" id="p40" style="--height:57.6042px;">My name is upon you, and my angels have charge over you.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note8" data-scroll-id="note8"><sup class="marker">8</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805239" id="p41" style="--height:28.8021px;">I will do wonders among you.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note9" data-scroll-id="note9"><sup class="marker">9</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805246" id="p42" style="--height:28.8021px;">Walk with me; learn of me; I will give you rest.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note10" data-scroll-id="note10"><sup class="marker">10</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805250" id="p43" style="--height:28.8021px;">I am in your midst.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note11" data-scroll-id="note11"><sup class="marker">11</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149808257" id="p44" style="--height:28.8021px;">You are mine.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note12" data-scroll-id="note12"><sup class="marker">12</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149808264" id="title4" style="--height:33.6111px;">To Those Who Are Surviving</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149808272" id="p11" style="--height:230.417px;">With those assurances very much in mind, I want to speak directly to those who feel as though there is no way out of their own survival story because of the trauma inflicted by the cruel actions of others. If this is your survival story, we weep with you. We yearn for you to overcome the confusion, shame, and fear, and we long for you, through Jesus Christ, to <em>conquer</em>.</p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149808280" id="title5" style="--height:67.2222px;">From Victim to Survivor to Conqueror</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149808289" id="p12" style="--height:144.01px;">If you have experienced any kind of abuse, violence, or oppression, you may be left with the idea that these events were somehow your fault and that you deserve to carry the shame and guilt you feel. You may have had thoughts such as:</p>
<ul class="bullet">
<li>
<p data-aid="149808299" id="p13" style="--height:28.8021px;">I could have prevented this.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p data-aid="149808308" id="p14" style="--height:28.8021px;">God doesn’t love me anymore.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p data-aid="149808317" id="p15" style="--height:28.8021px;">Nobody will ever love me.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p data-aid="149808328" id="p16" style="--height:28.8021px;">I am damaged beyond repair.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p data-aid="149808339" id="p17" style="--height:57.6042px;">The Savior’s Atonement applies to others but not to me.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-aid="149808347" id="p18" style="--height:230.417px;">These erroneous thoughts and feelings may have been a barrier to seeking help from family, friends, leaders, or professionals, and so you have struggled alone. If you have sought help from those you trust, you may still be wrestling with ideas of shame and even self-loathing. The impact of these events can remain for many years. You hope that one day you’ll feel better, but somehow that day has not yet come.</p>
<p data-aid="149808357" id="p19" style="--height:172.813px;">The abuse was not, is not, and never will be your fault, no matter what the abuser or anyone else may have said to the contrary. When you have been a victim of cruelty, incest, or any other perversion, you are not the one who needs to repent; you are not responsible.</p>
<p data-aid="149808367" id="p20" style="--height:86.4063px;">You are not less worthy or less valuable or less loved as a human being, or as a daughter or son of God, because of what someone else has done to you.</p>
<p data-aid="149808377" id="p21" style="--height:201.615px;">God does not now see, nor has He ever seen, you as someone to be <span class="page-break" data-page="39"></span>despised. Whatever has happened to you, He is <em>not</em> ashamed of you or disappointed in you. He loves you in a way you have yet to discover. And you <em>will</em> discover it as you trust in His promises and as you learn to believe Him when He says you are “<em>precious</em> in [His] sight.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note13" data-scroll-id="note13"><sup class="marker">13</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149808387" id="p22" style="--height:172.813px;">You are not defined by these terrible things that have been done to you. You are, in glorious truth, defined by your eternally existing identity as a son or daughter of God and by your Creator’s perfect, infinite love and invitation to whole and complete healing.</p>
<p data-aid="149808397" id="p23" style="--height:115.208px;">Though it may seem impossible, feel impossible, healing <em>can</em> come through the miracle of the redemptive might of the Atonement of Jesus Christ, who is risen “with healing in his wings.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note14" data-scroll-id="note14"><sup class="marker">14</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149808407" id="p24" style="--height:86.4063px;">Our merciful Savior, victorious over darkness and depravity, has power to right <em>all</em> wrongs, a life-giving truth for those wronged by others.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note15" data-scroll-id="note15"><sup class="marker">15</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149808417" id="p25" style="--height:259.219px;">Please know that the Savior has descended below <em>all</em> things, even what has happened to you. Because of that, He knows exactly what real terror and shame feel like and how it feels to be abandoned and broken.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note16" data-scroll-id="note16"><sup class="marker">16</sup></a> From the depths of His atoning suffering, the Savior imparts hope you thought was lost forever, strength you believed you could never possess, and healing you couldn’t imagine was possible.</p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149808428" id="title6" style="--height:100.833px;">Abusive Behavior Is Explicitly Condemned by the Lord and by His Prophets</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149808439" id="p26" style="--height:230.417px;">There is no place for any kind of abuse—physical, sexual, emotional, or verbal—in any home, any country, or any culture. Nothing a wife, child, or husband might do or say makes them “deserve” to be beaten. No one, in any country or culture, is ever “asking for” aggression or violence from someone else in authority or by someone who is bigger and stronger.</p>
<p data-aid="149808450" id="p27" style="--height:144.01px;">Those who abuse and who seek to hide their grievous sins may get away with it for a time. But the Lord, who sees all, knows the deeds and the thoughts and intents of the heart.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note17" data-scroll-id="note17"><sup class="marker">17</sup></a> He is a God of justice, and His divine justice will be served.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note18" data-scroll-id="note18"><sup class="marker">18</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149808461" id="p28" style="--height:172.813px;">Miraculously, the Lord is also a God of mercy to the truly repentant. Abusers—including those who were once abused themselves—who confess, forsake their sin, and do <em>all</em> in their power to make recompense and restitution, have access to forgiveness through the miracle of the Atonement of Christ.</p>
<p data-aid="149808473" id="p29" style="--height:144.01px;">For the falsely accused, the unspeakable gravity of these accusations brings its own purgatory. But they too are blessed by the Savior’s vicarious suffering for them and the knowledge that ultimately truth will prevail.</p>
<p data-aid="149808485" id="p30" style="--height:57.6042px;">But unrepentant abusers will stand before the Lord to account for their heinous crimes.</p>
<p data-aid="149808497" id="p31" style="--height:144.01px;">The Lord Himself is crystal clear in His condemnation of abuse of any kind: “But whoso shall offend one of these little ones&nbsp;…&nbsp;, it were better for him that a millstone were hanged about his neck, and that he were drowned in the depth of the sea.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note19" data-scroll-id="note19"><sup class="marker">19</sup></a></p>
</section>
<section>
<header>
<h2 data-aid="149808509" id="title7" style="--height:33.6111px;">Conclusion</h2>
</header>
<p data-aid="149808521" id="p32" style="--height:316.823px;">Dear friends who have been so terribly wounded—and for that matter, anyone who has borne the injustices of life—you can have a new beginning and a fresh start. In Gethsemane and on Calvary, Jesus “took upon Himself&nbsp;… <em>all</em> of the anguish and suffering <em>ever</em> experienced by you and me,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note20" data-scroll-id="note20"><sup class="marker">20</sup></a> and He has overcome it all! With arms outstretched, the Savior offers the gift of healing to you. With courage, patience, and faithful focus on Him, before too long you can come to fully accept this gift. You can let go of your pain and leave it at His feet.</p>
<p data-aid="149808533" id="p33" style="--height:201.615px;">Your gentle Savior declared, “The thief cometh not, but for to steal, and to kill, and to destroy: I am come that [you] might have life, and that [you] might have it more abundantly.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note21" data-scroll-id="note21"><sup class="marker">21</sup></a> You are a survivor, you can heal, and you can trust that with the power and grace of Jesus Christ, you will overcome and conquer.</p>
<p data-aid="149808545" id="p35" style="--height:201.615px;">Jesus specializes in the seemingly impossible. He came here to make the impossible possible, the irredeemable redeemable, to heal the unhealable, to right the unrightable, to promise the unpromisable.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/24kearon?lang=eng#note22" data-scroll-id="note22"><sup class="marker">22</sup></a> And He’s really good at it. In fact, He’s perfect at it. In the name of Jesus Christ, our Healer, amen.</p>
<p data-aid="149808557" id="p46" style="--height:86.4063px;"><em>For more information and resources, see “<a href="/study/life-help/abuse?lang=eng">Abuse</a>” in the Life Help section at ChurchofJesusChrist.org and in the Gospel Library app.</em></p>
</section>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149807425" id="p1" style="--height:115.208px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="40"></span>Speaking to Thomas&nbsp;B. Marsh, a recent convert, the Lord said encouragingly, “Lift up your heart and rejoice, for the hour of your mission is come” (<a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/dc-testament/dc/31.3?lang=eng#p3">Doctrine and Covenants 31:3</a>).</p>
<p data-aid="149807431" id="p2" style="--height:115.208px;">I believe this invitation can serve as an inspiration for all members of the Church. After all, we have each received from our Heavenly Father the mission of gathering Israel on both sides of the veil.</p>
<p data-aid="149807437" id="p3" style="--height:144.01px;">“That gathering,” President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson has said, “is the most important thing taking place on earth today. Nothing else compares in magnitude, nothing else compares in importance, nothing else compares in majesty.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/25aidukaitis?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807443" id="p4" style="--height:230.417px;">Certainly, there are many worthy causes in the world. It is impossible to name them all. But wouldn’t you like to participate in a great cause within your reach and where your contribution makes a vital difference? The gathering makes an eternal difference to all. People of all ages can participate in this cause regardless of their circumstances and where they live. <span class="page-break" data-page="41"></span>There is no other cause in the world more inclusive.</p>
<p data-aid="149807450" id="p5" style="--height:144.01px;">Speaking specifically to the youth, President Nelson said that “our Heavenly Father has reserved many of His most noble spirits—perhaps … His finest team—for this final phase. Those noble spirits—those finest players, those heroes—are <em>you</em>!”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/25aidukaitis?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807454" id="p6" style="--height:115.208px;">Yes, you have been prepared from before this life and born now to participate in the great work of the gathering of Israel on both sides of the veil in these latter days (see <a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/dc-testament/dc/138.53-56?lang=eng#p53">Doctrine and Covenants 138:53–56</a>).</p>
<p data-aid="149807460" id="p7" style="--height:288.021px;">Why is this cause so important? Because “the worth of souls is great in the sight of God” (<a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/dc-testament/dc/18.10?lang=eng#p10">Doctrine and Covenants 18:10</a>). And because “whoso believeth in [Jesus Christ], and is baptized, the same shall be saved; and … shall inherit the kingdom of God” (<a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/bofm/3-ne/11.33?lang=eng#p33">3&nbsp;Nephi 11:33</a>). Furthermore, “all that [the] Father hath shall be given unto” those who receive His ordinances and keep His covenants (<a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/dc-testament/dc/84.38?lang=eng#p38">Doctrine and Covenants 84:38</a>). In addition, “the labourers are few” (<a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/nt/luke/10.2?lang=eng#p2">Luke 10:2</a>).</p>
<p data-aid="149807466" id="p8" style="--height:115.208px;">Only in The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints do we find the power, the authority, and the way to offer such a blessing to others, whether living or dead.</p>
<p data-aid="149807472" id="p9" style="--height:172.813px;">As President Nelson said: “<em>Anytime</em> you do <em>anything</em> that helps <em>anyone</em>—on either side of the veil—take a step toward making covenants with God and receiving their essential baptismal and temple ordinances, you are helping to gather Israel. It is as simple as that.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/25aidukaitis?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807480" id="p10" style="--height:201.615px;">While there are many ways to help in the gathering, I would like to speak of one in particular: serving as a full-time missionary. For many of you, this will mean being a teaching missionary. For many others, it will mean being a service missionary. But the world tries to distract youth from this most sacred responsibility using fear and insecurities.</p>
<p data-aid="149807488" id="p11" style="--height:230.417px;">Some other distractions might be experiencing a pandemic, leaving a good job, putting off education, or being particularly interested in someone romantically. Everyone will have his or her own set of challenges. Such distractions can arise at precisely the time of embarking in the service of the Lord, and choices that seem obvious later are not always as easy in the moment.</p>
<p data-aid="149807496" id="p12" style="--height:201.615px;">I know from experience the troubled mind of such a young person. When I was preparing to go on my mission, some surprising forces tried to discourage me. One was my dentist. When he realized my appointment was so I could be a missionary, he tried to dissuade me from serving. I had not had the least notion that my dentist was against the Church.</p>
<p data-aid="149807502" id="p13" style="--height:230.417px;">The interruption of my education was also complicated. When I asked for a two-year leave of absence from my university program, I was informed that it was not possible. I would lose my place at the university if I did not return after one year. In Brazil, this was serious since the only criterion for admittance in a university program was a very difficult and competitive examination.</p>
<p data-aid="149807508" id="p14" style="--height:172.813px;">After repeatedly insisting, I was reluctantly informed that after being absent for one year, I could apply <span class="page-break" data-page="42"></span>for an exception on extraordinary grounds. It might be approved or not. I was terrified at the idea of retaking that difficult admissions test after two years away from my studies.</p>
<p data-aid="149807514" id="p15" style="--height:115.208px;">I also was especially interested in a young woman. Several of my friends shared that same interest. I thought to myself, “If I go on a mission, I’m running a risk.”</p>
<p data-aid="149807521" id="p16" style="--height:86.4063px;">But the Lord Jesus Christ was my great inspiration not to be afraid of the future as I strove to serve Him with all my heart.</p>
<p data-aid="149807528" id="p17" style="--height:288.021px;">He also had a mission to fulfill. In His own words, He explained, “For I came down from heaven, not to do mine own will, but the will of him that sent me” (<a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/nt/john/6.38?lang=eng#p38">John 6:38</a>). And was His mission easy? Of course not. His suffering, which was an essential part of His mission, caused Him, “even God, the greatest of all, to tremble because of pain, and to bleed at every pore, and to suffer both body and spirit—and would that [He] might not drink the bitter cup, and shrink—</p>
<p data-aid="149807536" id="p18" style="--height:115.208px;">“Nevertheless, glory be to the Father, and [He] partook and finished [His] preparations unto the children of men” (<a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/dc-testament/dc/19.18-19?lang=eng#p18">Doctrine and Covenants 19:18–19</a>).</p>
<p data-aid="149807545" id="p19" style="--height:115.208px;">Serving a full-time mission may seem difficult to us. Perhaps it requires that we give up important things for a moment. The Lord certainly knows this, and He will always be by our side.</p>
<p data-aid="149807554" id="p20" style="--height:201.615px;">In fact, in their message to missionaries in <em>Preach My Gospel</em>, the First Presidency promises, “The Lord will reward and richly bless you as you humbly and prayerfully serve Him.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/25aidukaitis?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a> It is true that all the children of God are blessed in one way or another, but there is a difference between being blessed and being richly blessed in His service.</p>
<p data-aid="149807563" id="p21" style="--height:144.01px;">Remember the challenges that I thought I faced prior to my mission? My dentist? I found another. My university? They made an exception for me. Remember that young woman? She married one of my good friends.</p>
<p data-aid="149807571" id="p22" style="--height:115.208px;">But God truly blessed me richly. And I learned that the blessings of the Lord can come in ways different from how we expect. After all, His thoughts are not our thoughts (see <a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/ot/isa/55.8-9?lang=eng#p8">Isaiah 55:8–9</a>).</p>
<p data-aid="149807581" id="p23" style="--height:432.031px;">Among the many rich blessings He has given me for serving Him as a full-time missionary are a greater faith in Jesus Christ and His Atonement and a stronger knowledge and testimony of His teachings, so that I am not easily swayed by “every wind of doctrine” (<a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/nt/eph/4.14?lang=eng#p14">Ephesians 4:14</a>). I lost my fear of teaching. My capacity to face challenges with optimism increased. By observing individuals and families I met or taught as a missionary, I learned that the teachings of God are true when He says that sin does not bring true happiness and that obedience to the commandments of God helps us prosper both temporally and spiritually (see <a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/bofm/mosiah/2.41?lang=eng#p41">Mosiah 2:41</a>; <a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/bofm/alma/41.10?lang=eng#p10">Alma 41:10</a>). And I learned for myself that God is a God of miracles (see <a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/bofm/morm/9?lang=eng">Mormon 9</a>).</p>
<p data-aid="149807590" id="p24" style="--height:115.208px;">All of these things were instrumental in my preparation for adult life, including possible marriage and parenthood, Church service, and professional and community life.</p>
<p data-aid="149807598" id="p25" style="--height:201.615px;">After my mission, I benefited from my increased courage to present myself as a faithful follower of Jesus Christ and His Church in all circumstances and to all people, even sharing the gospel with a beautiful woman who would become my virtuous, wise, fun, and beloved eternal companion, the sunshine of my life.</p>
<p data-aid="149807608" id="p26" style="--height:115.208px;">Yes, God has blessed me richly, far beyond what I imagined, just as He will all those who “humbly and prayerfully serve Him.” I am eternally grateful to God for His goodness.</p>
<p data-aid="149807617" id="p27" style="--height:144.01px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="43"></span>My mission completely shaped my life. I learned it is worth the effort to trust in God, to trust in His wisdom and mercy and in His promises. After all, He is our Father, and without any doubt, He wants the best for us.</p>
<p data-aid="149807626" id="p28" style="--height:144.01px;">Dear youth throughout the world, I extend the same invitation that our prophet, President Nelson, has made to all of you “to enlist in the youth battalion of the Lord to help gather Israel.” President Nelson said:</p>
<p data-aid="149807635" id="p32" style="--height:57.6042px;">“There is <em>nothing</em> of greater consequence. Absolutely <em>nothing</em>.</p>
<p data-aid="149807643" id="p31" style="--height:57.6042px;">“This gathering should mean <em>everything</em> to you. This <em>is</em> the mission for which you were sent to earth.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/25aidukaitis?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149807651" id="p29" style="--height:259.219px;">We were born at this time for a divine purpose, the gathering of Israel. When we serve as full-time missionaries, we will be challenged at times, but the Lord Himself is our great exemplar and guide in such circumstances. He understands what a difficult mission is. With His help, we can do hard things. He will be by our side (see <a class="scripture-ref" href="/study/scriptures/dc-testament/dc/84.88?lang=eng#p88">Doctrine and Covenants 84:88</a>), and He will bless us greatly as we humbly serve Him.</p>
<p data-aid="149807659" id="p30" style="--height:115.208px;">For all these reasons, I am not surprised that the Lord said to Thomas&nbsp;B. Marsh and to all of us, “Lift up your heart and rejoice, for the hour of your mission is come.” In the name of Jesus Christ, amen.</p>
</div>

<div class="body-block">
<p data-aid="149805175" id="p1" style="--height:86.4063px;">Friends, brothers and sisters, we each have a story. As we discover our story, we connect, we belong, we become.</p>
<p data-aid="149805179" id="p3" style="--height:86.4063px;">My name is Gerrit Walter Gong. Gerrit is a Dutch name, Walter (my father’s name) is an American name, and Gong of course is a Chinese name.</p>
<p data-aid="149805184" id="p4" style="--height:86.4063px;">Experts estimate some 70–110 billion people have lived on the earth. Perhaps only one has been named Gerrit Walter Gong.</p>
<p data-aid="149805189" id="p5" style="--height:172.813px;">We each have a story. I love “the rain on my face [and] the wind as it rushes by.”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note1" data-scroll-id="note1"><sup class="marker">1</sup></a> I wobble-waddle with penguins in Antarctica. I give orphans in Guatemala, street kids in Cambodia, Maasai women in the African Mara their first very own photo of themselves.</p>
<p data-aid="149805194" id="p6" style="--height:57.6042px;">I wait at the hospital as each of our children is born—once the doctor has me help.</p>
<p data-aid="149805199" id="p7" style="--height:86.4063px;">I trust God. I believe “[we] are, that [we] might have joy,”<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note2" data-scroll-id="note2"><sup class="marker">2</sup></a> that there are times and seasons to everything under heaven.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note3" data-scroll-id="note3"><sup class="marker">3</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805204" id="p8" style="--height:230.417px;">Do you know your story? What your name means? World population grew from 1.1 billion people in 1820 to nearly 7.8 billion in 2020.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note4" data-scroll-id="note4"><sup class="marker">4</sup></a> The year 1820 seems to be an inflection point in history. Many born after 1820 have living memory and records to identify several family generations. Can you think of a special, sweet memory with a grandparent or other family member?</p>
<p data-aid="149805210" id="p9" style="--height:86.4063px;">Whatever the total number of individuals who have lived on the earth, it is finite, countable, one person at a time. You and I, we each matter.</p>
<p data-aid="149805216" id="p10" style="--height:172.813px;">And please consider this: whether or not we know them, we are each born of a mother and father. And each mother and father is born of a mother and father.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note5" data-scroll-id="note5"><sup class="marker">5</sup></a> By birth or adoptive lineage, we are ultimately all connected in the family of God and in the human family.</p>
<p data-aid="149805223" id="p11" style="--height:144.01px;"><span class="page-break" data-page="44"></span>Born AD 837, my 30th great-grandfather, First Dragon Gong, started our family village in southern China. The first time I visited Gong village, the people said, “<em>Wenhan huilaile</em>” (“Gerrit has returned”).</p>
<p data-aid="149805229" id="p12" style="--height:259.219px;">On my mother’s side, our living family tree includes thousands of family names, with more to discover.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note6" data-scroll-id="note6"><sup class="marker">6</sup></a> We each have more family with whom to connect. If you think your great-aunt has completed all your family genealogy, please find your cousins and cousins’ cousins. Connect your living memory family names with the 10 billion searchable names FamilySearch now has in its online collection and the 1.3 billion individuals in its Family Tree.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note7" data-scroll-id="note7"><sup class="marker">7</sup></a></p>
<div><div class="imageWrapper-wTPPD"><figure class="imageWithModal-bCN6D loadImageItem-u5D4D" title="Tree"><img width="500" height="323" alt=""><div class="container-W4jed"><div class="innerFlex-R9N_u"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" role="presentation" style="width: 1.5rem; height: 1.5rem;"> <path fill="currentColor" d="M20 4.75L19.25 4v16l.75-.75H4l.75.75V4L4 4.75h16zM3.25 4v16c0 .414.336.75.75.75h16a.75.75 0 0 0 .75-.75V4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75-.75H4a.75.75 0 0 0-.75.75zm11.07 8.888c.23-.357.606-.353.828-.008l2.887 4.482c.227.352.06.638-.357.638H6.326c-.421 0-.581-.3-.37-.648l4.006-6.622c.217-.358.567-.359.793.014l2.396 3.96 1.17-1.816zm1.59-2.735c1.14 0 2.066-.907 2.066-2.026 0-1.12-.926-2.027-2.067-2.027s-2.066.907-2.066 2.027c0 1.119.925 2.026 2.066 2.026z"> </path></svg><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr i18nString-raclU">Image</div><div class="sc-1szn76m-0 dODiQr title-RrK9J">Tree</div></div></div></figure></div></div>
<p data-aid="149805236" id="p13" style="--height:172.813px;">Ask friends or family to draw a living tree. As President Russell&nbsp;M. Nelson teaches, living trees have roots <em>and</em> branches.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note8" data-scroll-id="note8"><sup class="marker">8</sup></a> Whether you are your first or tenth known generation, connect yesterday for tomorrow. Connect the roots and branches in your living family tree.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note9" data-scroll-id="note9"><sup class="marker">9</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805243" id="p14" style="--height:172.813px;">The question “Where are you from?” asks lineage, birthplace, and home country or homeland. Globally, 25 percent of us trace our homeland to China, 23 percent to India, 17 percent to other parts of Asia and the Pacific, 18 percent to Europe, 10 percent to Africa, 7 percent to the Americas.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note10" data-scroll-id="note10"><sup class="marker">10</sup></a></p>
<p data-aid="149805251" id="p15" style="--height:86.4063px;">The question “Where are you from?” also invites us to discover our divine identity and spiritual purpose in life.</p>
<p data-aid="149808258" id="p16" style="--height:28.8021px;">We each have a story.</p>
<p data-aid="149808265" id="p17" style="--height:172.813px;">A family I know connected five family generations when they visited their old home in Winnipeg, Canada. There the grandfather told his grandsons about the day two missionaries (he called them angels from heaven) brought the restored gospel of Jesus Christ, changing their family forever.</p>
<p data-aid="149808273" id="p18" style="--height:144.01px;">A mother I know invited her children and their cousins to ask their great-grandmother about her childhood experiences. Great-Grandma’s adventures and life lessons are now a treasured family book uniting generations.</p>
<p data-aid="149808282" id="p19" style="--height:144.01px;">A young man I know is compiling a “Dad journal.” Years ago, a car hit and killed his father. Now, to know his father, this courageous young man is preserving childhood memories and stories from family and friends.</p>
<p data-aid="149808291" id="p20" style="--height:144.01px;">When asked where meaning comes in life, most people rank <em>family</em> first.<a class="note-ref" href="/study/general-conference/2022/04/26gong?lang=eng#note11" data-scroll-id="note11"><sup class="marker">11</sup></a> This includes family living and gone before.
